Catch Victoria Harbour’s Glow Watch the Symphony of Lights at 8 pm from Tsim Sha Tsui’s Avenue of Stars— with Bruce Lee and Maggie Cheung statues—as skyscraper beams dazzle Victoria Harbour. Ride the Star Ferry for a close-up shine or relax on West Kowloon’s waterfront lawn to see cargo ships glide by. It’s Hong Kong’s nightly spectacle. 7. Explore Theme Parks Visit Hong Kong Disneyland—Ant-Man and The Wasp: Nano Battle! Zips you through, Mystic Manor twists with oddities, and fireworks burst over the Castle of Magical Dreams. Try Ocean Park—ride Hair Raiser or Flash’s vertical drop, see shark tanks and pandas, plus hit Water World’s 27-meter slides in summer. Both are easy to reach by MTR. 8. Hike Wild Trails Trek Dragon’s Back—ridge trails drop to Shek O’s glassy sea in 2.5-3.5 hours, with surfers dotting below; bring HK$20 for the bus return.\nTry MacLehose Trail’s Section 2—white sands lead to Po Pin Chau’s hexagonal sea stacks, accessible only at low tide (check HK Observatory app). Both weave through hills with stunning coastal views. 9. Visit the Big Buddha Ride Ngong Ping 360’s cable cars to Lantau—glass floors show the hills below—leading to the 26.4m Big Buddha (34m with lotus base). Nearby, stroll through Tai O’s stilted fishing village; book boat tours to pink dolphin zones. Enjoy Po Lin Monastery’s calm and veggie meals for a peaceful day above the city hum. 10. Cycle Island Escapes Ferry from Central to Cheung Chau—bike car-free lanes from Kwun Yam Beach to Pak Tai Temple’s old carvings (rentals near ferry pier). Or roll through Lamma Island’s fishing villages—seafood shacks line Yung Shue Wan. The 30-minute rides open quiet paths and sea breezes beyond the skyline. 11.\nStroll Heritage Trails Walk the Ping Shan Heritage Trail from Tin Shui Wai MTR—ancient walls, Hong Kong’s only ancient three-story Tsui Sing Lau Pagoda, and ancestral halls trace centuries. Add Kam Tin’s Kat Hing Wai walled village—stone gates guard Hakka history. It’s a quiet step into Hong Kong’s rural roots. 12. Relax on the Beaches Take a bus from Central to Repulse Bay Beach—it will take you 30 minutes to get to the soft sand, calm waves, and hillside mansions. Try Stanley Main Beach—livelier tides near a Tin Hau shrine and weekend markets. Both swap urban grind for sun-soaked shores and a quick dip. 13. Ride the Urban Escalator Ride the Central–Mid-Levels Escalator—the world’s longest outdoor covered system at 800 meters—uphill to Mid-Levels from 10am-midnight (downhill 6-10am). Stop in Soho for coffee, then walk down past wet markets. It’s a smooth lift through Hong Kong’s buzz.\n\n...\n\n## Things to do in Hong Kong\n### What to do\nLooking for things to do in Hong Kong? ## Hong Kong Disneyland Highlights: Must-See Features and Attractions

Some information may have been translated by Google Translate

**Join a Magical Party Like No Other at the Hong Kong Disneyland 20th Anniversary!**

On a magical island away from the rest of the world, we're throwing a party that could only happen in front of the Castle of Magical Dreams. With magic! And hosted by all your favorite Disney Friends, dressed in spectacular 20th Anniversary-only party outfits, who are hosting this star-studded event. From the skies above to the air all around, across every stage, street, and corner, glitz and glam radiate across this land of seemingly endless celebration. Get ready to fill your world with jubilation and celebration like never before, as you get closer than ever to Disney magic at the party of all parties.

Hong Kong Disneyland 20th Anniversary celebration until Jun 7, 2026, calling for all Disney fans to enjoy the party! Visit now!

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo1u12000k60t9gy7523_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

  

**All-New Anniversary-Only Castle Stage Show**

Kick things off with a bang! Get ready to bob your heads and join our hosts, Mickey and Friends, Duffy and Friends, and Disney Princesses, for a limited-time, one-year-only, electrifying celebration with music, dancing, and visual theatrics. Feel the energy of beloved Disney Friends in an exhilarating daytime performance that will leave you ready to party like never before.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo2q12000m3wcf57ACD1_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

  

**All-New “Friendtastic!” Parade**

Get the party moving! Rise to meet the excitement of our all-new, long-anticipated, and largest-ever parade, featuring 11 floats that come alive with kinetic energy, and 11 groups of beloved Disney Friends who can't wait to see you. Jump into an empowering party vibe bursting with spectacular theatrics, positive energy, and toe-tapping beats designed to get you on your feet.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo1112000k60sf6280E7_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

  

**A Special 20th Anniversary Edition of “Momentous”**

The Most Magical Show On Earth will become even more magical. With even more stories, majestic projections that extend down the entire length of Main Street U.S.A, and magically inspired drone choreography, the upgraded nighttime spectacular is the unforgettable climax to the ultimate day-to-night party.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo3o12000k60vimvD9EC_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

The Magical Party Never Stops

Dress to impress! Mickey and Friends and Duffy and Friends will appear in highly-anticipated 20th Anniversary-only outfits.

Camera ready? Capture picture-perfect moments you can't wait to share with special décor across the resort.

Indulge in crave-worthy, time-limited F&B and merchandise items, refreshed throughout the year.

Party day and night at our 3 hotels with themed décor, exhilarating activities, and enchanting hospitality.

  

  

**WORLD OF FROZEN IS NOW OPEN AT HONG KONG DISNEYLAND**

"For the First Time in Forever," immerse yourself fully in the epic world of the beloved "Frozen" films, brought to life before your very eyes!

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo4o12000dbkr5kp3464_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

**Let It Go Like Never Before at World of Frozen**

Guests are invited to explore the kingdom of Arendelle, from a magical musical boat ride to zooming through Arendelle's picturesque landscape, and Anna and Elsa's hidden forest hideaway. Indulge yourself in delicious cuisine, pick up unique souvenirs, delve deeper into the story of “Frozen” with enchanting attractions and experiences in day and night!

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo6512000dbkrmc44EE8_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo4412000cdcuzfa8539_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

**THE MOST MAGICAL SHOW ON EARTH**

The nighttime spectacular, “Momentous”, illuminates the night sky with about 20 minutes of music and memorable moments. It reminds us how precious time is, and to cherish every moment with our loved ones.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/01004120009xe630d8500_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

**CASTLE OF MAGICAL DREAMS**

Standing as a shining beacon of courage, hope and possibility, the Castle of Magical Dreams stands proudly as the new centerpiece of Hong Kong Disneyland. It is built on 13 classic Disney tales of Princesses and Queens and inspires everyone to dream big.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo4b12000bbbc7pu9690_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

**IT'S PLAYTIME WITH DUFFY AND FRIENDS**

Are you ready to jump into a whole new Fans-tasy adventure? Duffy and Friends are dressed in their seasonal outfits, and they want to write new stories with you! They love to spend this colorful time surrounded by laughter, smelling the flowers, touching the grass, bouncing around, jumping for joy, and playing wherever and whenever with you! So, let your innocent self out to play wholeheartedly.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo1t12000dbkroh5F7D3_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

**CAN'T MISS MARVEL EXPERIENCES**

If you are a Marvel fan, be sure to join the heroes in defeating the evil forces of Hydra at the highly-rated Iron Man Experience, and Ant-Man and The Wasp: Nano-Battle!

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo1q12000b74qi4v9590_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

Fantastic Dining And Shopping Experiences

Feast your eyes and satisfy your appetite with a whimsical assortment of food items inspired by classic Disney Characters or taste the exquisite cuisine integrating authentic flavors from around the world; and bring back a keepsake or two from the merchandise store to commemorate the magical experience.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo6s12000dbkrn25287F_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

Stay In The Magic

Extend the Disney spirit for a never-ending magical experience at Hong Kong Disneyland Resort hotels. Whether you are vacationing in a themed suite, spending a romantic staycation, or celebrating a spectacular day. The happiest place on earth becomes the dreami-est place, the delicious-est place, the magic-est place, with iconic Disney Friends at every turn.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo5a12000dbkrmci6D66_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

## Additional information

### Admission restrictions

Dress code

Guests over the age of 16 are not allowed to wear costumes. If the park deems the clothing to be inappropriate or may affect the play experience of other guests, the park reserves the right to refuse entry to the park or require the inappropriate clothing to be removed. Guests over the age of 16 are not allowed to wear face coverings (except for medical masks). If younger guests wear a face covering, the face covering must not obstruct peripheral vision at all times, and the position of the eyes must be completely clear and unobstructed.

Other restrictions

The park will check guests' bags when they enter the park. Drinks and chemicals in glass bottles cannot be brought into the park. Each guest is limited to bringing a small amount of food, such as a pack of biscuits and a pack of bread.

\*The above information is for reference only. Please refer to the actual information provided by the attraction.

Catch Victoria Harbour’s Glow Watch the Symphony of Lights at 8 pm from Tsim Sha Tsui’s Avenue of Stars— with Bruce Lee and Maggie Cheung statues—as skyscraper beams dazzle Victoria Harbour. Ride the Star Ferry for a close-up shine or relax on West Kowloon’s waterfront lawn to see cargo ships glide by. It’s Hong Kong’s nightly spectacle. 7. Explore Theme Parks Visit Hong Kong Disneyland—Ant-Man and The Wasp: Nano Battle! Zips you through, Mystic Manor twists with oddities, and fireworks burst over the Castle of Magical Dreams. Try Ocean Park—ride Hair Raiser or Flash’s vertical drop, see shark tanks and pandas, plus hit Water World’s 27-meter slides in summer. Both are easy to reach by MTR. 8. Hike Wild Trails Trek Dragon’s Back—ridge trails drop to Shek O’s glassy sea in 2.5-3.5 hours, with surfers dotting below; bring HK$20 for the bus return.\nTry MacLehose Trail’s Section 2—white sands lead to Po Pin Chau’s hexagonal sea stacks, accessible only at low tide (check HK Observatory app). Both weave through hills with stunning coastal views. 9. Visit the Big Buddha Ride Ngong Ping 360’s cable cars to Lantau—glass floors show the hills below—leading to the 26.4m Big Buddha (34m with lotus base). Nearby, stroll through Tai O’s stilted fishing village; book boat tours to pink dolphin zones. Enjoy Po Lin Monastery’s calm and veggie meals for a peaceful day above the city hum. 10. Cycle Island Escapes Ferry from Central to Cheung Chau—bike car-free lanes from Kwun Yam Beach to Pak Tai Temple’s old carvings (rentals near ferry pier). Or roll through Lamma Island’s fishing villages—seafood shacks line Yung Shue Wan. The 30-minute rides open quiet paths and sea breezes beyond the skyline. 11.\n\n...\n\n### Hong Kong Travel Tips\n1. Plan Around Temple Street Night Market’s Rhythm Temple Street Night Market in Kowloon kicks off after 6 p.m.—trinkets, street food, fortune tellers—but shuts Mondays for cleanup. Hit Tuesday or Friday; weekends pack tight by 8 p.m., so slide in earlier to dodge the crush. Bring small bills—vendors lean cash over cards. 2. Secure Peak Tram Tickets Ahead The Peak Tram to Victoria Peak means up to 60 minute waits—or longer—in peak times like October or Chinese New Year. Book online a day or two ahead for a timed slot; early rides around sunrise catch the haze lifting off the skyline. Spare morning? The nearby Morning Trail’s a scenic dodge if lines drag. 3. Navigate Public Transport Like a Local Hong Kong’s MTR is fast and spotless—snag an Octopus card at stations (small deposit, reloadable) for trains, buses, even convenience stores. On escalators, stand right, walk left—same for the Mid-Levels Escalator—or you’ll jam the flow.\n\n...\n\n## Things to do in Hong Kong\n### What to do\nLooking for things to do in Hong Kong? ## Hong Kong Disneyland Highlights: Must-See Features and Attractions

**Join a Magical Party Like No Other at the Hong Kong Disneyland 20th Anniversary!**

On a magical island away from the rest of the world, we're throwing a party that could only happen in front of the Castle of Magical Dreams. With magic! And hosted by all your favorite Disney Friends, dressed in spectacular 20th Anniversary-only party outfits, who are hosting this star-studded event. From the skies above to the air all around, across every stage, street, and corner, glitz and glam radiate across this land of seemingly endless celebration. Get ready to fill your world with jubilation and celebration like never before, as you get closer than ever to Disney magic at the party of all parties.

Hong Kong Disneyland 20th Anniversary celebration until Jun 7, 2026, calling for all Disney fans to enjoy the party! Visit now!

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo1u12000k60t9gy7523_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

  

**All-New Anniversary-Only Castle Stage Show**

Kick things off with a bang! Get ready to bob your heads and join our hosts, Mickey and Friends, Duffy and Friends, and Disney Princesses, for a limited-time, one-year-only, electrifying celebration with music, dancing, and visual theatrics. Feel the energy of beloved Disney Friends in an exhilarating daytime performance that will leave you ready to party like never before.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo2q12000m3wcf57ACD1_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

  

**All-New “Friendtastic!” Parade**

Get the party moving! Rise to meet the excitement of our all-new, long-anticipated, and largest-ever parade, featuring 11 floats that come alive with kinetic energy, and 11 groups of beloved Disney Friends who can't wait to see you. Jump into an empowering party vibe bursting with spectacular theatrics, positive energy, and toe-tapping beats designed to get you on your feet.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo1112000k60sf6280E7_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

  

**A Special 20th Anniversary Edition of “Momentous”**

The Most Magical Show On Earth will become even more magical. With even more stories, majestic projections that extend down the entire length of Main Street U.S.A, and magically inspired drone choreography, the upgraded nighttime spectacular is the unforgettable climax to the ultimate day-to-night party.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo3o12000k60vimvD9EC_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

The Magical Party Never Stops

Dress to impress! Mickey and Friends and Duffy and Friends will appear in highly-anticipated 20th Anniversary-only outfits.

Camera ready? Capture picture-perfect moments you can't wait to share with special décor across the resort.

Indulge in crave-worthy, time-limited F&B and merchandise items, refreshed throughout the year.

Party day and night at our 3 hotels with themed décor, exhilarating activities, and enchanting hospitality.

  

  

**WORLD OF FROZEN IS NOW OPEN AT HONG KONG DISNEYLAND**

"For the First Time in Forever," immerse yourself fully in the epic world of the beloved "Frozen" films, brought to life before your very eyes!

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo4o12000dbkr5kp3464_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

**Let It Go Like Never Before at World of Frozen**

Guests are invited to explore the kingdom of Arendelle, from a magical musical boat ride to zooming through Arendelle's picturesque landscape, and Anna and Elsa's hidden forest hideaway. Indulge yourself in delicious cuisine, pick up unique souvenirs, delve deeper into the story of “Frozen” with enchanting attractions and experiences in day and night!

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo6512000dbkrmc44EE8_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo4412000cdcuzfa8539_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

**THE MOST MAGICAL SHOW ON EARTH**

The nighttime spectacular, “Momentous”, illuminates the night sky with about 20 minutes of music and memorable moments. It reminds us how precious time is, and to cherish every moment with our loved ones.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/01004120009xe630d8500_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

**CASTLE OF MAGICAL DREAMS**

Standing as a shining beacon of courage, hope and possibility, the Castle of Magical Dreams stands proudly as the new centerpiece of Hong Kong Disneyland. It is built on 13 classic Disney tales of Princesses and Queens and inspires everyone to dream big.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo4b12000bbbc7pu9690_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

**IT'S PLAYTIME WITH DUFFY AND FRIENDS**

Are you ready to jump into a whole new Fans-tasy adventure? Duffy and Friends are dressed in their seasonal outfits, and they want to write new stories with you! They love to spend this colorful time surrounded by laughter, smelling the flowers, touching the grass, bouncing around, jumping for joy, and playing wherever and whenever with you! So, let your innocent self out to play wholeheartedly.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo1t12000dbkroh5F7D3_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

**CAN'T MISS MARVEL EXPERIENCES**

If you are a Marvel fan, be sure to join the heroes in defeating the evil forces of Hydra at the highly-rated Iron Man Experience, and Ant-Man and The Wasp: Nano-Battle!

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo1q12000b74qi4v9590_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

Fantastic Dining And Shopping Experiences

Feast your eyes and satisfy your appetite with a whimsical assortment of food items inspired by classic Disney Characters or taste the exquisite cuisine integrating authentic flavors from around the world; and bring back a keepsake or two from the merchandise store to commemorate the magical experience.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo6s12000dbkrn25287F_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

Stay In The Magic

Extend the Disney spirit for a never-ending magical experience at Hong Kong Disneyland Resort hotels. Whether you are vacationing in a themed suite, spending a romantic staycation, or celebrating a spectacular day. The happiest place on earth becomes the dreami-est place, the delicious-est place, the magic-est place, with iconic Disney Friends at every turn.

## Additional information

### Admission restrictions

Dress code

Guests over the age of 16 are not allowed to wear costumes. If the park deems the clothing to be inappropriate or may affect the play experience of other guests, the park reserves the right to refuse entry to the park or require the inappropriate clothing to be removed. Guests over the age of 16 are not allowed to wear face coverings (except for medical masks). If younger guests wear a face covering, the face covering must not obstruct peripheral vision at all times, and the position of the eyes must be completely clear and unobstructed.

Other restrictions

The park will check guests' bags when they enter the park. Drinks and chemicals in glass bottles cannot be brought into the park. Each guest is limited to bringing a small amount of food, such as a pack of biscuits and a pack of bread.

\*The above information is for reference only. Please refer to the actual information provided by the attraction.

## Hong Kong Disneyland Highlights: Must-See Features and Attractions

Some information may have been translated by Google Translate

**Join a Magical Party Like No Other at the Hong Kong Disneyland 20th Anniversary!**

On a magical island away from the rest of the world, we're throwing a party that could only happen in front of the Castle of Magical Dreams. With magic! And hosted by all your favorite Disney Friends, dressed in spectacular 20th Anniversary-only party outfits, who are hosting this star-studded event. From the skies above to the air all around, across every stage, street, and corner, glitz and glam radiate across this land of seemingly endless celebration. Get ready to fill your world with jubilation and celebration like never before, as you get closer than ever to Disney magic at the party of all parties.

Hong Kong Disneyland 20th Anniversary celebration until Jun 7, 2026, calling for all Disney fans to enjoy the party! Visit now!

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo1u12000k60t9gy7523_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

  

**All-New Anniversary-Only Castle Stage Show**

Kick things off with a bang! Get ready to bob your heads and join our hosts, Mickey and Friends, Duffy and Friends, and Disney Princesses, for a limited-time, one-year-only, electrifying celebration with music, dancing, and visual theatrics. Feel the energy of beloved Disney Friends in an exhilarating daytime performance that will leave you ready to party like never before.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo2q12000m3wcf57ACD1_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

  

**All-New “Friendtastic!” Parade**

Get the party moving! Rise to meet the excitement of our all-new, long-anticipated, and largest-ever parade, featuring 11 floats that come alive with kinetic energy, and 11 groups of beloved Disney Friends who can't wait to see you. Jump into an empowering party vibe bursting with spectacular theatrics, positive energy, and toe-tapping beats designed to get you on your feet.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo1112000k60sf6280E7_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

  

**A Special 20th Anniversary Edition of “Momentous”**

The Most Magical Show On Earth will become even more magical. With even more stories, majestic projections that extend down the entire length of Main Street U.S.A, and magically inspired drone choreography, the upgraded nighttime spectacular is the unforgettable climax to the ultimate day-to-night party.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo3o12000k60vimvD9EC_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

The Magical Party Never Stops

Dress to impress! Mickey and Friends and Duffy and Friends will appear in highly-anticipated 20th Anniversary-only outfits.

Camera ready? Capture picture-perfect moments you can't wait to share with special décor across the resort.

Indulge in crave-worthy, time-limited F&B and merchandise items, refreshed throughout the year.

Party day and night at our 3 hotels with themed décor, exhilarating activities, and enchanting hospitality.

  

  

**WORLD OF FROZEN IS NOW OPEN AT HONG KONG DISNEYLAND**

"For the First Time in Forever," immerse yourself fully in the epic world of the beloved "Frozen" films, brought to life before your very eyes!

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo4o12000dbkr5kp3464_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

**Let It Go Like Never Before at World of Frozen**

Guests are invited to explore the kingdom of Arendelle, from a magical musical boat ride to zooming through Arendelle's picturesque landscape, and Anna and Elsa's hidden forest hideaway. Indulge yourself in delicious cuisine, pick up unique souvenirs, delve deeper into the story of “Frozen” with enchanting attractions and experiences in day and night!

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo6512000dbkrmc44EE8_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo4412000cdcuzfa8539_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

**THE MOST MAGICAL SHOW ON EARTH**

The nighttime spectacular, “Momentous”, illuminates the night sky with about 20 minutes of music and memorable moments. It reminds us how precious time is, and to cherish every moment with our loved ones.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/01004120009xe630d8500_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

**CASTLE OF MAGICAL DREAMS**

Standing as a shining beacon of courage, hope and possibility, the Castle of Magical Dreams stands proudly as the new centerpiece of Hong Kong Disneyland. It is built on 13 classic Disney tales of Princesses and Queens and inspires everyone to dream big.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo4b12000bbbc7pu9690_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

**IT'S PLAYTIME WITH DUFFY AND FRIENDS**

Are you ready to jump into a whole new Fans-tasy adventure? Duffy and Friends are dressed in their seasonal outfits, and they want to write new stories with you! They love to spend this colorful time surrounded by laughter, smelling the flowers, touching the grass, bouncing around, jumping for joy, and playing wherever and whenever with you! So, let your innocent self out to play wholeheartedly.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo1t12000dbkroh5F7D3_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

**CAN'T MISS MARVEL EXPERIENCES**

If you are a Marvel fan, be sure to join the heroes in defeating the evil forces of Hydra at the highly-rated Iron Man Experience, and Ant-Man and The Wasp: Nano-Battle!

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo1q12000b74qi4v9590_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

Fantastic Dining And Shopping Experiences

Feast your eyes and satisfy your appetite with a whimsical assortment of food items inspired by classic Disney Characters or taste the exquisite cuisine integrating authentic flavors from around the world; and bring back a keepsake or two from the merchandise store to commemorate the magical experience.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo6s12000dbkrn25287F_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

Stay In The Magic

Extend the Disney spirit for a never-ending magical experience at Hong Kong Disneyland Resort hotels. The happiest place on earth becomes the dreami-est place, the delicious-est place, the magic-est place, with iconic Disney Friends at every turn.

## Additional information

### Admission restrictions

Dress code

Guests over the age of 16 are not allowed to wear costumes. If the park deems the clothing to be inappropriate or may affect the play experience of other guests, the park reserves the right to refuse entry to the park or require the inappropriate clothing to be removed. Guests over the age of 16 are not allowed to wear face coverings (except for medical masks). If younger guests wear a face covering, the face covering must not obstruct peripheral vision at all times, and the position of the eyes must be completely clear and unobstructed.

Other restrictions

The park will check guests' bags when they enter the park. Drinks and chemicals in glass bottles cannot be brought into the park. Each guest is limited to bringing a small amount of food, such as a pack of biscuits and a pack of bread.

\*The above information is for reference only. Please refer to the actual information provided by the attraction.

**Join a Magical Party Like No Other at the Hong Kong Disneyland 20th Anniversary!**

On a magical island away from the rest of the world, we're throwing a party that could only happen in front of the Castle of Magical Dreams. With magic! And hosted by all your favorite Disney Friends, dressed in spectacular 20th Anniversary-only party outfits, who are hosting this star-studded event. From the skies above to the air all around, across every stage, street, and corner, glitz and glam radiate across this land of seemingly endless celebration. Get ready to fill your world with jubilation and celebration like never before, as you get closer than ever to Disney magic at the party of all parties.

Hong Kong Disneyland 20th Anniversary celebration until Jun 7, 2026, calling for all Disney fans to enjoy the party! Visit now!

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo1u12000k60t9gy7523_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

  

**All-New Anniversary-Only Castle Stage Show**

Kick things off with a bang! Get ready to bob your heads and join our hosts, Mickey and Friends, Duffy and Friends, and Disney Princesses, for a limited-time, one-year-only, electrifying celebration with music, dancing, and visual theatrics. Feel the energy of beloved Disney Friends in an exhilarating daytime performance that will leave you ready to party like never before.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo2q12000m3wcf57ACD1_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

  

**All-New “Friendtastic!” Parade**

Get the party moving! Rise to meet the excitement of our all-new, long-anticipated, and largest-ever parade, featuring 11 floats that come alive with kinetic energy, and 11 groups of beloved Disney Friends who can't wait to see you. Jump into an empowering party vibe bursting with spectacular theatrics, positive energy, and toe-tapping beats designed to get you on your feet.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo1112000k60sf6280E7_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

  

**A Special 20th Anniversary Edition of “Momentous”**

The Most Magical Show On Earth will become even more magical. With even more stories, majestic projections that extend down the entire length of Main Street U.S.A, and magically inspired drone choreography, the upgraded nighttime spectacular is the unforgettable climax to the ultimate day-to-night party.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo3o12000k60vimvD9EC_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

The Magical Party Never Stops

Dress to impress! Mickey and Friends and Duffy and Friends will appear in highly-anticipated 20th Anniversary-only outfits.

Camera ready? Capture picture-perfect moments you can't wait to share with special décor across the resort.

Indulge in crave-worthy, time-limited F&B and merchandise items, refreshed throughout the year.

Party day and night at our 3 hotels with themed décor, exhilarating activities, and enchanting hospitality.

"For the First Time in Forever," immerse yourself fully in the epic world of the beloved "Frozen" films, brought to life before your very eyes!

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo6512000dbkrmc44EE8_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

### Admission restrictions

Guests over the age of 16 are not allowed to wear face coverings (except for medical masks). If younger guests wear a face covering, the face covering must not obstruct peripheral vision at all times, and the position of the eyes must be completely clear and unobstructed.

Other restrictions

**Join a Magical Party Like No Other at the Hong Kong Disneyland 20th Anniversary!**

On a magical island away from the rest of the world, we're throwing a party that could only happen in front of the Castle of Magical Dreams. With magic! And hosted by all your favorite Disney Friends, dressed in spectacular 20th Anniversary-only party outfits, who are hosting this star-studded event. From the skies above to the air all around, across every stage, street, and corner, glitz and glam radiate across this land of seemingly endless celebration. Get ready to fill your world with jubilation and celebration like never before, as you get closer than ever to Disney magic at the party of all parties.

Hong Kong Disneyland 20th Anniversary celebration until Jun 7, 2026, calling for all Disney fans to enjoy the party! Visit now!

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo1u12000k60t9gy7523_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

  

**All-New Anniversary-Only Castle Stage Show**

Kick things off with a bang! Get ready to bob your heads and join our hosts, Mickey and Friends, Duffy and Friends, and Disney Princesses, for a limited-time, one-year-only, electrifying celebration with music, dancing, and visual theatrics. Feel the energy of beloved Disney Friends in an exhilarating daytime performance that will leave you ready to party like never before.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo2q12000m3wcf57ACD1_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

  

**All-New “Friendtastic!” Parade**

Get the party moving! Rise to meet the excitement of our all-new, long-anticipated, and largest-ever parade, featuring 11 floats that come alive with kinetic energy, and 11 groups of beloved Disney Friends who can't wait to see you. Jump into an empowering party vibe bursting with spectacular theatrics, positive energy, and toe-tapping beats designed to get you on your feet.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo1112000k60sf6280E7_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

  

**A Special 20th Anniversary Edition of “Momentous”**

The Most Magical Show On Earth will become even more magical. With even more stories, majestic projections that extend down the entire length of Main Street U.S.A, and magically inspired drone choreography, the upgraded nighttime spectacular is the unforgettable climax to the ultimate day-to-night party.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo3o12000k60vimvD9EC_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

The Magical Party Never Stops

Dress to impress! Mickey and Friends and Duffy and Friends will appear in highly-anticipated 20th Anniversary-only outfits.

Camera ready? Capture picture-perfect moments you can't wait to share with special décor across the resort.

Indulge in crave-worthy, time-limited F&B and merchandise items, refreshed throughout the year.

Party day and night at our 3 hotels with themed décor, exhilarating activities, and enchanting hospitality.

  

  

**WORLD OF FROZEN IS NOW OPEN AT HONG KONG DISNEYLAND**

"For the First Time in Forever," immerse yourself fully in the epic world of the beloved "Frozen" films, brought to life before your very eyes!

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo4o12000dbkr5kp3464_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

**Let It Go Like Never Before at World of Frozen**

Guests are invited to explore the kingdom of Arendelle, from a magical musical boat ride to zooming through Arendelle's picturesque landscape, and Anna and Elsa's hidden forest hideaway. Indulge yourself in delicious cuisine, pick up unique souvenirs, delve deeper into the story of “Frozen” with enchanting attractions and experiences in day and night!

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo6512000dbkrmc44EE8_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo4412000cdcuzfa8539_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

**THE MOST MAGICAL SHOW ON EARTH**

The nighttime spectacular, “Momentous”, illuminates the night sky with about 20 minutes of music and memorable moments. It reminds us how precious time is, and to cherish every moment with our loved ones.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/01004120009xe630d8500_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

**CASTLE OF MAGICAL DREAMS**

Standing as a shining beacon of courage, hope and possibility, the Castle of Magical Dreams stands proudly as the new centerpiece of Hong Kong Disneyland. It is built on 13 classic Disney tales of Princesses and Queens and inspires everyone to dream big.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo4b12000bbbc7pu9690_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

**IT'S PLAYTIME WITH DUFFY AND FRIENDS**

Are you ready to jump into a whole new Fans-tasy adventure? Duffy and Friends are dressed in their seasonal outfits, and they want to write new stories with you! They love to spend this colorful time surrounded by laughter, smelling the flowers, touching the grass, bouncing around, jumping for joy, and playing wherever and whenever with you! So, let your innocent self out to play wholeheartedly.

**CAN'T MISS MARVEL EXPERIENCES**

If you are a Marvel fan, be sure to join the heroes in defeating the evil forces of Hydra at the highly-rated Iron Man Experience, and Ant-Man and The Wasp: Nano-Battle!

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo1q12000b74qi4v9590_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo6s12000dbkrn25287F_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

## Additional information

### Admission restrictions

Dress code

Guests over the age of 16 are not allowed to wear costumes. If the park deems the clothing to be inappropriate or may affect the play experience of other guests, the park reserves the right to refuse entry to the park or require the inappropriate clothing to be removed. Guests over the age of 16 are not allowed to wear face coverings (except for medical masks). If younger guests wear a face covering, the face covering must not obstruct peripheral vision at all times, and the position of the eyes must be completely clear and unobstructed.

Other restrictions

The park will check guests' bags when they enter the park. Drinks and chemicals in glass bottles cannot be brought into the park. Each guest is limited to bringing a small amount of food, such as a pack of biscuits and a pack of bread.

\*The above information is for reference only. Please refer to the actual information provided by the attraction.

## Hong Kong Disneyland attraction highlights

Some information may have been translated by Google Translate

**Join a Magical Party Like No Other at the Hong Kong Disneyland 20th Anniversary!**

On a magical island away from the rest of the world, we're throwing a party that could only happen in front of the Castle of Magical Dreams. With magic! And hosted by all your favorite Disney Friends, dressed in spectacular 20th Anniversary-only party outfits, who are hosting this star-studded event. From the skies above to the air all around, across every stage, street, and corner, glitz and glam radiate across this land of seemingly endless celebration. Get ready to fill your world with jubilation and celebration like never before, as you get closer than ever to Disney magic at the party of all parties.

Hong Kong Disneyland 20th Anniversary celebration until Jun 7, 2026, calling for all Disney fans to enjoy the party! Visit now!

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo1u12000k60t9gy7523_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

  

**All-New Anniversary-Only Castle Stage Show**

Kick things off with a bang! Get ready to bob your heads and join our hosts, Mickey and Friends, Duffy and Friends, and Disney Princesses, for a limited-time, one-year-only, electrifying celebration with music, dancing, and visual theatrics. Feel the energy of beloved Disney Friends in an exhilarating daytime performance that will leave you ready to party like never before.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo2q12000m3wcf57ACD1_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

  

**All-New “Friendtastic!” Parade**

Get the party moving! Rise to meet the excitement of our all-new, long-anticipated, and largest-ever parade, featuring 11 floats that come alive with kinetic energy, and 11 groups of beloved Disney Friends who can't wait to see you. Jump into an empowering party vibe bursting with spectacular theatrics, positive energy, and toe-tapping beats designed to get you on your feet.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo1112000k60sf6280E7_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

  

**A Special 20th Anniversary Edition of “Momentous”**

The Most Magical Show On Earth will become even more magical. With even more stories, majestic projections that extend down the entire length of Main Street U.S.A, and magically inspired drone choreography, the upgraded nighttime spectacular is the unforgettable climax to the ultimate day-to-night party.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo3o12000k60vimvD9EC_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

The Magical Party Never Stops

Dress to impress! Mickey and Friends and Duffy and Friends will appear in highly-anticipated 20th Anniversary-only outfits.

Camera ready? Capture picture-perfect moments you can't wait to share with special décor across the resort.

Indulge in crave-worthy, time-limited F&B and merchandise items, refreshed throughout the year.

Party day and night at our 3 hotels with themed décor, exhilarating activities, and enchanting hospitality.

  

  

**WORLD OF FROZEN IS NOW OPEN AT HONG KONG DISNEYLAND**

"For the First Time in Forever," immerse yourself fully in the epic world of the beloved "Frozen" films, brought to life before your very eyes!

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo4o12000dbkr5kp3464_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

**Let It Go Like Never Before at World of Frozen**

Guests are invited to explore the kingdom of Arendelle, from a magical musical boat ride to zooming through Arendelle's picturesque landscape, and Anna and Elsa's hidden forest hideaway. Indulge yourself in delicious cuisine, pick up unique souvenirs, delve deeper into the story of “Frozen” with enchanting attractions and experiences in day and night!

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo6512000dbkrmc44EE8_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo4412000cdcuzfa8539_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

**THE MOST MAGICAL SHOW ON EARTH**

The nighttime spectacular, “Momentous”, illuminates the night sky with about 20 minutes of music and memorable moments. It reminds us how precious time is, and to cherish every moment with our loved ones.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/01004120009xe630d8500_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

**CASTLE OF MAGICAL DREAMS**

Standing as a shining beacon of courage, hope and possibility, the Castle of Magical Dreams stands proudly as the new centerpiece of Hong Kong Disneyland. It is built on 13 classic Disney tales of Princesses and Queens and inspires everyone to dream big.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo4b12000bbbc7pu9690_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

**IT'S PLAYTIME WITH DUFFY AND FRIENDS**

Are you ready to jump into a whole new Fans-tasy adventure? Duffy and Friends are dressed in their seasonal outfits, and they want to write new stories with you! They love to spend this colorful time surrounded by laughter, smelling the flowers, touching the grass, bouncing around, jumping for joy, and playing wherever and whenever with you! So, let your innocent self out to play wholeheartedly.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo1t12000dbkroh5F7D3_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

**CAN'T MISS MARVEL EXPERIENCES**

If you are a Marvel fan, be sure to join the heroes in defeating the evil forces of Hydra at the highly-rated Iron Man Experience, and Ant-Man and The Wasp: Nano-Battle!

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo1q12000b74qi4v9590_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

Fantastic Dining And Shopping Experiences

Feast your eyes and satisfy your appetite with a whimsical assortment of food items inspired by classic Disney Characters or taste the exquisite cuisine integrating authentic flavors from around the world; and bring back a keepsake or two from the merchandise store to commemorate the magical experience.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo6s12000dbkrn25287F_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

Stay In The Magic

Extend the Disney spirit for a never-ending magical experience at Hong Kong Disneyland Resort hotels. Whether you are vacationing in a themed suite, spending a romantic staycation, or celebrating a spectacular day. The happiest place on earth becomes the dreami-est place, the delicious-est place, the magic-est place, with iconic Disney Friends at every turn.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo5a12000dbkrmci6D66_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo5a12000dbkr7jcD73A_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo4212000dbkr4enA56E_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

## Additional information

### Admission restrictions

Dress code

Guests over the age of 16 are not allowed to wear costumes. If the park deems the clothing to be inappropriate or may affect the play experience of other guests, the park reserves the right to refuse entry to the park or require the inappropriate clothing to be removed. Guests over the age of 16 are not allowed to wear face coverings (except for medical masks). If younger guests wear a face covering, the face covering must not obstruct peripheral vision at all times, and the position of the eyes must be completely clear and unobstructed.

Other restrictions

The park will check guests' bags when they enter the park. Drinks and chemicals in glass bottles cannot be brought into the park. Each guest is limited to bringing a small amount of food, such as a pack of biscuits and a pack of bread.

\*The above information is for reference only. Please refer to the actual information provided by the attraction.

**Join a Magical Party Like No Other at the Hong Kong Disneyland 20th Anniversary!**

On a magical island away from the rest of the world, we're throwing a party that could only happen in front of the Castle of Magical Dreams. With magic! And hosted by all your favorite Disney Friends, dressed in spectacular 20th Anniversary-only party outfits, who are hosting this star-studded event. From the skies above to the air all around, across every stage, street, and corner, glitz and glam radiate across this land of seemingly endless celebration. Get ready to fill your world with jubilation and celebration like never before, as you get closer than ever to Disney magic at the party of all parties.

Hong Kong Disneyland 20th Anniversary celebration until Jun 7, 2026, calling for all Disney fans to enjoy the party! Visit now!

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo1u12000k60t9gy7523_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

  

**All-New Anniversary-Only Castle Stage Show**

Kick things off with a bang! Get ready to bob your heads and join our hosts, Mickey and Friends, Duffy and Friends, and Disney Princesses, for a limited-time, one-year-only, electrifying celebration with music, dancing, and visual theatrics. Feel the energy of beloved Disney Friends in an exhilarating daytime performance that will leave you ready to party like never before.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo2q12000m3wcf57ACD1_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

  

**All-New “Friendtastic!” Parade**

Get the party moving! Rise to meet the excitement of our all-new, long-anticipated, and largest-ever parade, featuring 11 floats that come alive with kinetic energy, and 11 groups of beloved Disney Friends who can't wait to see you. Jump into an empowering party vibe bursting with spectacular theatrics, positive energy, and toe-tapping beats designed to get you on your feet.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo1112000k60sf6280E7_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

  

**A Special 20th Anniversary Edition of “Momentous”**

The Most Magical Show On Earth will become even more magical. With even more stories, majestic projections that extend down the entire length of Main Street U.S.A, and magically inspired drone choreography, the upgraded nighttime spectacular is the unforgettable climax to the ultimate day-to-night party.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo3o12000k60vimvD9EC_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

The Magical Party Never Stops

Dress to impress! Mickey and Friends and Duffy and Friends will appear in highly-anticipated 20th Anniversary-only outfits.

Camera ready? Capture picture-perfect moments you can't wait to share with special décor across the resort.

Indulge in crave-worthy, time-limited F&B and merchandise items, refreshed throughout the year.

Party day and night at our 3 hotels with themed décor, exhilarating activities, and enchanting hospitality.

"For the First Time in Forever," immerse yourself fully in the epic world of the beloved "Frozen" films, brought to life before your very eyes!

Guests are invited to explore the kingdom of Arendelle, from a magical musical boat ride to zooming through Arendelle's picturesque landscape, and Anna and Elsa's hidden forest hideaway. Indulge yourself in delicious cuisine, pick up unique souvenirs, delve deeper into the story of “Frozen” with enchanting attractions and experiences in day and night!

The nighttime spectacular, “Momentous”, illuminates the night sky with about 20 minutes of music and memorable moments. It reminds us how precious time is, and to cherish every moment with our loved ones.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/01004120009xe630d8500_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

**CASTLE OF MAGICAL DREAMS**

Standing as a shining beacon of courage, hope and possibility, the Castle of Magical Dreams stands proudly as the new centerpiece of Hong Kong Disneyland. It is built on 13 classic Disney tales of Princesses and Queens and inspires everyone to dream big.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo4b12000bbbc7pu9690_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

**IT'S PLAYTIME WITH DUFFY AND FRIENDS**

Are you ready to jump into a whole new Fans-tasy adventure? Duffy and Friends are dressed in their seasonal outfits, and they want to write new stories with you! So, let your innocent self out to play wholeheartedly.

## Additional information

### Admission restrictions

Dress code

Guests over the age of 16 are not allowed to wear costumes. If the park deems the clothing to be inappropriate or may affect the play experience of other guests, the park reserves the right to refuse entry to the park or require the inappropriate clothing to be removed. Guests over the age of 16 are not allowed to wear face coverings (except for medical masks). If younger guests wear a face covering, the face covering must not obstruct peripheral vision at all times, and the position of the eyes must be completely clear and unobstructed.

Other restrictions

The park will check guests' bags when they enter the park. Drinks and chemicals in glass bottles cannot be brought into the park. Each guest is limited to bringing a small amount of food, such as a pack of biscuits and a pack of bread.

\*The above information is for reference only. Please refer to the actual information provided by the attraction.

Re: What to do near Disneyland?\n3 years ago\nSave\nWell, there are indeed (mildly) interesting things to see on Lantau Island , but the realities of transportation (slow buses or taxis to get around on Lantau, compared to fast MTR connection downtown) mean that it is almost surely much more convenient to just go downtown, visit the shopping malls or explore the Mid-Levels escalator and Sheung Wan, and find a bite to eat. For first-timers in HK, these activities offer much more of interest than the artificial creations (cable car, village, Buddha statue) on Lantau.\nBy the way, in terms of nice parks, the waterfront park along the Central and Wanchai harbourfront is a great option -- it is pedestrian-friendly and the views are unbeatable. You can just exit from the MTR Hong Kong Station and easily walk from there. Assuming, of course, that the weather is okay.\nReply\nReport inappropriate content\nThanksSocialSecurity\nDublin, California\n39,685 posts\n18 helpful votes\n4. Re: What to do near Disneyland?\n3 years ago\nSave\nGeographically near doesn't mean convenient to get to - Disney to DB is easily 45 mins or more. Hong Kong Island and Kowloon may be closer, time wise. Disney hotel to Big Buddha will take well over an hour, even if taking taxi all the way.\nThe ferry from Central used to run in the morning to Disney, and a couple hours later back to Central. Obviously not meant as transport as such, more as a scenic leisure trip.\nFor your one non-Disney day, take the MTR to the city for exploring, returning sometime in the evening. There's basically nothing out at Disney other than Disney.\nReply\nReport inappropriate content\nSammyFD\nHong Kong, China\nDestination Expert\nfor Hong Kong, Osaka, Tokyo\n85,760 posts\n192 helpful votes\n6. Re: What to do near Disneyland?\n3 years ago\nSave\nOther than NP360 and Po Lin Monastery, I don't think other attractions on Lantau Island are worthy. Tai O is a small fishing village but I didn't find it very interesting. It does depend on whether you have gone to similar villages anywhere in the world. Discovery Bay is decent but it's not really a visitor destination. You can go there, walk around and chill out at a waterfront restaurant. Citygate is just a smallish outlet mall.\nMy suggestion is you just take the MTR to anywhere you find interesting in the city.\nReply\nReport inappropriate content\nJosietak\n8 posts\n7. Log into your account\nyour username\nyour password\nForgot your password? Get help\nPrivacy Policy\nPassword recovery\nRecover your password\nyour email\nA password will be e-mailed to you. Home Destinations Asia\n    * Asia\n    * Hong Kong\n\nThe Ultimate Hong Kong Disneyland Guide (2025): Secrets, Tips & Must-Dos\nBy Nicole Varella\n- January 7, 2025\nThe hoi-sumest place on earth to let it go! ❄️\nWhen I first visited Hong Kong Disneyland a decade ago, I was underwhelmed. It seemed like a watered-down, almost pirated version of Disney magic. So when the park became part of our 7D Hong Kong trip , my reaction was a solid “meh”. But now, the attractions are nothing short of world-class, and you can’t help feeling that sense of wonder. I say this as a full-grown adult, so you know it must be true! And the good news is they just keep building bigger and better attractions.\nPhoto credit: @hkdisneyland via Instagram\nCase in point: the long-awaited World of Frozen just opened back in November 2023! The kingdom of Arendelle is ready to explore with familiar sights from the movie like the ice palace, the clock tower, and the friendship fountain. Not to mention, Hong Kong Disneyland also unveiled its Castle of Magic Dreams in 2020, featuring 14 Disney princesses! You’ll also find attractions not found in any other Disneyland, like the first-ever Marvel ride  (on top of a Marvel land in the works ) and a unique spin on the Haunted Mansion . Click to jump to each section: Changes in operations | Pre-visit tips | Difference among tickets | Getting to HK Disneyland | Must-do rides and shows | Exclusive secrets | Suggested routes | Must-eats | FAQs\nChanges in operations Opening hours: Generally 10:30AM – 8:30PM (Mon – Thu), 10AM – 9PM (Fri – Sun). From September 2023 onwards, the park is closed every Wed (except PH and certain days).\nCheck the opening hours before going. Before visiting:\n– All guests must reserve a slot for their visit on the Hong Kong Disneyland website prior to arrival, up to 90 days in advance. This includes tickets purchased via Klook . – Check here for the updated list of attractions and shows for each day. – Download the Hong Kong Disneyland mobile app to check attraction wait times. Stickers: Cast members no longer give out free stickers post-Covid 🙁\nPre-visit tips\n1) Avoid visiting during peak periods To avoid crowds, steer clear of weekends,  school holidays and China’s Golden Week holidays . It’s also best to visit during the cooler months of October to April (bonus: this period includes Halloween and Christmas decor and festivities). 2) Pre-book tickets to save money and skip the queue Save % by booking through Klook . A one-day pass can go from  ~S$109 , compared to the HK$669 ( ~S$117 ) price tag on the official site .\n\n...\n\nThe cheapest (and most scenic) transport option is the MTR. Take the Tung Chung Line to Sunny Bay Station, transfer to the Disneyland Resort Line and onto the Disney train. It’s hard to miss, with adorable Disney-themed handles and memorabilia! If you’re coming from the airport, it’s a 20-minute taxi ride which costs ~HK$180 (~S$31). Read also:   Ultimate Hong Kong Guide — 28 Must-Sees, Hidden Gems, And Everything In Between\nMust-Do Rides and Shows at Hong Kong Disneyland Here’s what you can’t miss in each of the eight themed lands. Attractions and Must-Dos in World of Frozen Photo credit: Hong Kong Disneyland\nThe Norwegian-inspired World of Frozen is based on the Summer Snowy Day celebration, which hardcore fans of the movie know as the day Anna saved Elsa from death. While Arendelle isn’t open yet, here’s what you can expect based on what we know so far! Must-Dos\n1) Frozen Ever After: An immersive boat ride in Elsa’s Ice Palace featuring characters and songs from the Frozen movies.\nFrozen Ever After . Photo credit: Hong Kong Disneyland\n2) Wandering Oaken’s Sliding Sleighs: A family-friendly coaster that takes you through the Arendelle Forest. Wandering Oaken’s Sliding Sleighs . Photo credit: Hong Kong Disneyland\n3) Playhouse in the Woods: A play set in the Arendelle Forest where Anna and Elsa return to their childhood hideaway and Elsa’s magic powers will be on display. Attractions and Must-Dos on Main Street, USA Designed like a 20th-century American town, Main Street, USA is where the, well, main action happens, with key parades and guest utilities. Walking through this area is like entering the Lady and the Tramp ‘s idyllic scenes, a throwback to simpler days gone by. Must-Dos\n1)  Hong Kong Disneyland Railroad : A scenic train ride with a last stop at Fantasyland, the furthest end of the park. 2) “Momentous” Nighttime Spectacular : A light and fireworks show that debuted in June 2022 — featuring almost 150 Disney and Pixar characters.\nThis 20-minute show is the last attraction after all the other rides have closed and gets crowded fast . Secure good viewing spots at least 30 minutes before showtime! *Pro-tip: We recommend the corner near the gantry, which also lets you quickly exit the park! Other Attractions\n3)  Animation Academy : A 20-minute class on drawing your favourite Disney characters. While instructions are in Cantonese, the steps are easy enough to follow. You can even take your masterpiece home! 4)  Art of Animation : An exhibit with storyboards, paintings, and a cool zoetrope machine for a behind-the-scenes look at Disney animation. Photo credit: Hong Kong Disneyland\n5) Pixar Water Play Street Party : A daytime parade with huge floats and your favourite Pixar characters — Buzz Lightyear, Mr and Mrs Incredible, Frozone and more! 6)  Main Street Vehicles : A one-way drive down Main Street in a charming vintage automobile. 7) The Royal Reception Hall : Meet Cinderella, Belle and more!\n\n...\n\n4)  Wild West Photo Fun : Quirky photo spots including a Wanted poster, jail cell, and a huge golden nugget! Attractions and Must-Dos in  Mystic Point  Mystic Point takes you to the tropical wilderness of Papua New Guinea, where supernatural forces come into play. Its highlight: An intimidating Victorian manor, home of eccentric Lord Henry Mystic and his cheeky monkey, Albert . Must-Dos\n1)  Mystic Manor : Without a doubt, the best ride in the entire park! If you’ve only got time for one thing in Hong Kong Disneyland, this is it. Mystic Manor’s ride design is built like  Disney’s Haunted Mansion , but the similarities end there. This Hong Kong Disneyland-exclusive comes with a unique story, adorable characters, and an immersive experience that’s full of surprises. This family-friendly ride doesn’t have many thrills, but more than makes up for it with special effects and storytelling. Even adults will want seconds on this one! Mystic Manor.\n\n...\n\n5)  Toy Soldier Boot Camp : An interactive show where toy soldiers train young volunteers for battle. You’ll find them at the entrance of Toy Story Land, next to the statue of Woody — check with cast members for exact timings. Toy Soldier Boot Camp. Attractions and Must-Dos in  Fantasyland  Fantasyland brings classic fairytales to life, with dreamy decor and classic carnival rides. Must-Dos\n1) Castle of Magical Dreams: To commemorate its 15th anniversary, Hong Kong Disneyland unveiled a new Castle of Magical Dreams in November 2020. This castle celebrates 14 of our favourite Disney princesses — like Belle and Elsa! 2)  Mickey and the Wondrous Book : The best show in Hong Kong Disneyland. The 30-minute spectacle brings Disney stories to life with innovative musical mashups. Mickey and the Wondrous Book. *Pro-tip:  Arrive at least 15 minutes early to secure the best seats — at the centre and near the back, where you can see all the action and read the English subtitles easily.\n\n...\n\n3) Ant-Man and The Wasp: Nano Battle : Step into the tiny shoes of Ant-Man and fight alongside him and the Wasp to stop Hydra in this exciting shooting ride. Other Attractions\n4)  Orbitron : Pilot your own spaceship through a galaxy of planets. This ride’s best taken at night, when the planets light up in a neon blaze. Orbitron\n5)  Iron Man Tech Showcase : For a photo with the charismatic superhero himself. Secrets & tips for Hong Kong Disneyland 1) [NEW] Use Disney Premier Access for the popular attractions Photo credit: Hong Kong Disneyland\nHong Kong Disneyland no longer uses the free FASTPASS system — you’ll now have to purchase Disney Premier Access ( available via Klook add-on ) to skip the queues instead. It pretty much works the same, where you’ll have to scan your Disney Premier Access QR code at each attraction to enjoy priority access. You can purchase either Disney Premier Access for a single attraction, or a bundle of three or eight attractions.\n\n...\n\nShows always include English translations, and there’s never a point where I didn’t understand what was going on. 2) Should I stay at a hotel near Hong Kong Disneyland? Photo credit: Hong Kong Disneyland\nSince the park is so accessible by public transport, it’s not crucial to stay onsite. However, there are some cool benefits, like the walking-distance proximity to Disneyland, and special  character dining opportunities . Level up your magical experience at one of the three hotels: the grand  Hong Kong Disneyland Hotel , Art Deco-inspired  Disney’s Hollywood Hotel , and jungle-themed  Disney Explorers Lodge . *Pro-tip: Check out Klook’s Stay+ deals — discounted bundles when you book a hotel and add on travel essentials or attraction tickets (including Hong Kong Disneyland!) While a trip to Hong Kong Disneyland is a lot more uncomplicated than a trip to Walt Disney World or Tokyo Disney Resort, it still requires a bit of planning so you don’t just run around the park like a chicken with its head cut off in the blazing Hong Kong heat. Attractions Guide Conclusion\n\n...\n\n## **Can’t Miss Attractions**\n### **Mystic Manor**\nWhat transpires after is a whirlwind adventure filled with tension, laughs, and eye-popping sight gags that are sure to leave a lasting impression. With its plethora of rooms and set pieces, from dart-shooting tikis to head-chopping suits of armor, the attraction succeeds in telling a complete story that incorporates variety into its design.\nSince that side of the park doesn’t open until about 30 minutes to one hour after the rest of the park opens, I would recommend going on this a bit later in the day and prioritizing the Toy Story Land attractions or Big Grizzly Mountain Runaway Mine Cars first. However, if you want to ride this multiple times and the rides at Toy Story Land don’t interest you, I’d recommend doing Big Grizzly Mountain first then heading here to ride it multiple times.\n\n...\n\n### **Momentous**\nThat being said, unless you’re visiting during a holiday or during peak season, it should be easy to get a viewing spot at the hub or on Main Street. There are also experiences, restaurant reservations, and premier access packages that include access to a reserved viewing area right in front of the castle. They cost extra, naturally, but might be worth it for you if you’re only going to be there for a day. That being said, be at Main Street or the hub as early as you can during peak season, as there was one time on a trip during the height of summer that I got to Main Street 15 minutes before showtime and struggled to find a spot.\n\n...\n\n### Friendtastic Parade\nThe best place to watch the show from would be the performance corridor in between Tomorrowland and Fantasyland. The hub near Adventureland and Town Square are also great places to watch it from. I would arrive 15-20 minutes before showtime, and maybe even earlier on busy days, to get a good spot for the parade. Remember, don’t have your umbrella open during the show as doing so is considered rude.\n\n...\n\n### **Hyperspace Mountain**\n**[Hong Kong Disneyland Dining Offers](https://klook.tpm.li/9lcIRTFk)**\n[**Hong Kong Disneyland Hotel**](https://klook.tpm.li/CrPw7hf6)\n**[Disney Explorers Lodge](https://klook.tpm.li/XKSd3yKW)**\n**[Disney’s Hollywood Hotel](https://klook.tpm.li/mHxofW0S)**\n\n...\n\n### **Mickey’s Philharmagic**\nRating: A-\nThe classic 3D show has been a staple of Hong Kong Disneyland since opening in 2005. While the title is a little misleading given that Donald is the star of the show, and while its use of 3D is kind of an outdated novelty at this point, it’s still a very fun romp through the worlds of Disney animation.\nThe HKDL version now has the new Coco scene, which will further cement it as one of the best Hong Kong Disneyland attractions. The queue and the waiting area feel quintessentially Fantasyland, and since the theater was made with the show in mind, the scents and effects make this show come alive in a very visceral way\nThis show rarely gets a line and your wait will depend on if the next show has just started or is nearing its end. If you catch it right as it’s about to end, you probably won’t end up waiting for it that long. If you catch it just as it begins, however, you’re going to have to wait till the show cycles through to the next show.\n\n...\n\n## Hong Kong Disneyland Rides and Attractions Guide Conclusion\nThe best Hong Kong Disneyland attractions can be considered some of the best attractions in the world. Then this post is for you! While a trip to Hong Kong Disneyland is a lot more uncomplicated than a trip to Walt Disney World or Tokyo Disney Resort, it still requires a bit of planning so you don’t just run around the park like a chicken with its head cut off in the blazing Hong Kong heat. One of those things you need to consider and plan for when visiting HKDL is which attractions are worth your time and which aren’t. You’ve got to know what the best Hong Kong Disneyland attractions and rides are so you know which attractions to commit your time to. Which is where this Hong Kong Disneyland Rides and Attractions Guide comes in handy.\nAll in all, HKDL has over 30 attractions, shows, and rides for you to enjoy. For the purposes of this post, I will only be talking about actual rides, attractions, and shows, not theming elements that HKDL considers as attractions like the Liki Tikis or Geyser Gulch. While those are fine experiences and they definitely add to the lands they’re in, I don’t think anyone would consider them real attractions.\nI will be going over each attraction briefly, starting from the best Hong Kong Disneyland rides and attractions to the not-so-great ones, to help you discern and figure out which ones you should prioritize on your next trip. As a rule of thumb, every attraction that gets a B+ or higher can be considered one of the best Hong Kong Disneyland attractions and one that you shouldn’t miss.\n\n...\n\n* Can’t Miss Attractions\n+ Mystic Manor\n+ Momentous\n+ Big Grizzly Mountain Runaway Mine Cars\n+ Mickey and the Wondrous Book\n+ Festival of the Lion King\n+ Friendtastic Parade\n+ Frozen Ever After\n+ It’s a Small World\n+ The Many Adventures of Winnie the Pooh\n+ Jungle River Cruise\n+ Hyperspace Mountain\n+ Iron Man Experience\n+ Mickey’s Philharmagic\n+ Fairy Tale Forest\n+ Wandering Oaken’s Sliding Sleighs\n+ Ant-Man and the Wasp Nano Battle\n+ Follow Your Dreams\n* The Rest of the Pack\n+ Playhouse in the Woods\n+ Moana: A Homecoming Celebration\n+ RC Racer\n+ Hong Kong Disneyland Railroad\n+ Tarzan’s Treehouse\n+ Animation Academy\n+ Duffy and Friends Playhouse\n+ Orbitron\n+ Toy Soldier Parachute Drop\n+ Slinky Dog Spin\n+ Dumbo the Flying Elephant\n+ Cinderella Carousel\n+ Mad Hatter Tea Cups\n+ Main Street Vehicles\n* Hong Kong Disneyland Rides and Attractions Guide Conclusion\n\n...\n\n## **Can’t Miss Attractions**\n### **Momentous**\nRating: A+\nAn epic show on a grand scale that will surely leave you not only breathless but with a tear in your eye. Featuring engaging projections and a captivating musical score, Momentous ranks up there with Happily Ever After, Remember…Dreams Come True, Disney Dreams, Wondrous Journeys, and Illuminations: Reflections of Earth as one of the greatest Disney nighttime spectaculars of all time. It’s also, in my opinion, the second best Hong Kong Disneyland attraction, which is why it’s the only other attraction other than Mystic Manor to get an A+ in this Hong Kong Disneyland rides and attractions guide.\nIts story is simple. It chronicles all the major life milestones of the human experience, from birth to death, benchmarked by Disney songs that relate to those big life moments. It’s a concept never seen before, and one that will leave you with your jaw agape. It’s the perfect way to end a day at HKDL.\n\n...\n\n### **Big Grizzly Mountain Runaway Mine Cars**\nIn the attraction, you embark on a tour of the Big Grizzly Mountain Mines when, all of a sudden, a family of bears that live in the mountains derail your tour and send you careening across the entire land. Featuring a backwards section and a launch, this coaster packs a lot of thrills and surprises with an interesting story and cuddly protagonists. The story is original, just like Mystic Manor, and is a hallmark of 2010s imagineering. It’s one of the best Hong Kong Disneyland rides and attractions and takes inspiration from other Disney rides such as Big Thunder Mountain at Disneyland and Expedition Everest at Animal Kingdom.\n\n...\n\n### **Iron Man Experience**\nRating: A-\nDisney’s first Marvel themed ride, the Iron Man Experience is an exciting romp through Hong Kong as you join forces with Tony Stark to save the city from a HYDRA invasion. The minute you step into the ride’s fantastic queue, you’re immersed in the world of Iron Man. Showcasing models of different Iron Wings, as well as a full size Iron Man suit, you’re then quickly whisked away into the latest Iron Wing and then take off from Stark Expo to see the new Arc Reactor that is at the top of Stark Tower in downtown Hong Kong.\nHydra, however, invades Hong Kong in an effort to steal the Arc Reactor. What follows is a thrilling battle between Iron Man and your Iron Wing and Hydra. While it isn’t innovative like Millenium Falcon: Smugglers Run and doesn’t have the randomized scenes like Star Tours, it still tells a compelling and exciting story and is a major part of the Hong Kong Disneyland rides and attractions lineup.\n\n...\n\n## **The Rest of the Pack**\n### **Duffy and Friends Playhouse**\nRating: B\nA walkthrough attraction on the left side of the end of Main Street, this walkthrough allows you to meet Duffy and his friends in a setting that resembles one of those toontown houses located in Disneyland and Tokyo Disneyland.\nWhile it’s a big draw if you’re a Duffy fan, I wouldn’t enter if you aren’t as the lines to get through the whole thing can get pretty long. Do this as soon as it opens if you’re interested in it.\n\n...\n\n## Hong Kong Disneyland Rides and Attractions Guide Conclusion\n1 [2](https://thedisneyspecialist.com/hong-kong-disneyland-attraction-and-ride-guide/page/2/) [Next](https://thedisneyspecialist.com/hong-kong-disneyland-attraction-and-ride-guide/page/2/)\nLoad More Posts"],"source_id":"search_e6620f9535bf40b8a8146e5fceaf0451#4"},{"url":"https://www.hongkongdisneyland.com/zh-hk/id/attractions/","title":"香港迪士尼樂園","excerpts":["# Attractions\nAdventures, classic stories and exhilarating thrills.\n所有樂園及酒店\n位置\n* 所有樂園及酒店\n  主題樂園\n* 香港迪士尼樂園\n  其他目的地\n* 迪欣湖活動中心\n  酒店\n* 迪士尼好萊塢酒店\n* 迪士尼探索家度假酒店\n* 香港迪士尼樂園酒店\n清除 - 所有樂園及酒店\n所有活動 遊樂設施 餐飲 娛樂表演 節慶及主題活動 樂園便利服務 酒店 樂園及目的地 休閒娛樂 商店 觀光服務  遊樂設施 currently selected. 1.  所有活動\n2.  遊樂設施\n3.  餐飲\n4.  娛樂表演\n5.  節慶及主題活動\n6.  樂園便利服務\n7.  酒店\n8.  樂園及目的地\n9.  休閒娛樂\n10.  商店\n11.  觀光服務\n搜尋遊樂設施\nsearchBox.clearButton.text searchBox.searchButton.text\n45 項遊樂設施\nDate\n Selected date, Thursday, April 16, 2026. 介绍

香港迪士尼乐园**20周年奇妙派对**

在香港迪士尼乐园，来一场奇妙的派对！一般你喜爱的迪士尼朋友将悉心打扮，以由梦想构建的城堡为中心，于整个乐园呈献星光闪闪的庆祝派对。亮丽迷人的光彩将从空中绽放到每个舞台、街道与角落，并蔓延到你身上，让你大放异彩，令这场盛况空前的派对更加奇妙。约定你，一齐参与香港迪士尼乐园20周年庆祝派对！

香港迪士尼乐园20周年庆典将于今年6月7日圆满收官，迪士尼粉丝快来打卡，把特别的20周年快乐留住！

![](https://dimg04.c-ctrip.com/images/1lo1u12000k60t9gy7523.jpg)

**全新周年限定城堡演出**

为派对来一个热热闹闹的开场！由米奇与好友、Duffy与好友及迪士尼公主组成的迪士尼星级阵容呈献，集合派对音乐与精彩舞蹈的视听享受，带来一场只上演一年的限定日间城堡演出。

![](https://dimg04.c-ctrip.com/images/1lo2q12000m3wcf57ACD1.jpg)

**全新「Friendtastic!」巡游表演**

让派对动起来！11架派对巡游花车，11组迪士尼朋友，会在这场万众期待、乐园开幕以来大型的全新巡游表演中，一起瞩目登场，将充满活力与正能量的派对气氛散播到整条美国小镇大街，让大家都跟著跳起舞来。

![](https://dimg04.c-ctrip.com/images/1lo1112000k60sf6280E7.jpg)

  

**「迪士尼星梦光影之旅」20周年限定版**

「迪士尼星梦光影之旅」将变得更加奇妙！夜间城堡汇演将新增更多故事片段、延伸至整条美国小镇大街的沉浸式投影，以及满布亮点的无人机演出，为日夜连场的派对绽放难忘一幕。

![](https://dimg04.c-ctrip.com/images/1lo3o12000k60vimvD9EC.jpg)

  

**不停派对 奇妙庆祝！**

一齐为派对悉心打扮！米奇与好友将联同Duffy与好友换上的20周年限定服装亮相，就连乐园四处的装饰都换上新面貌，和你的打扮一样瞩目，准备不停打卡！

派对礼遇

周年限定的美食与周边商品亦全年不断上架，让你由乐园到酒店又食又买，同时享受三间迪士尼酒店的主题布置、特别活动与精心款待，日夜派对！

  

  

**魔雪奇缘世界**

已于香港迪士尼乐园正式开幕

"For the First Time in Forever"，宾客可以置身在壮阔的《魔雪奇缘》电影世界，让一个个熟悉的电影场景，现在都成为你眼前的风景！

![](https://dimg04.c-ctrip.com/images/1lo4o12000dbkr5kp3464.jpg)

## Hong Kong Disneyland attraction highlights
