**Join a Magical Party Like No Other at the Hong Kong Disneyland 20th Anniversary!**

On a magical island away from the rest of the world, we're throwing a party that could only happen in front of the Castle of Magical Dreams. With magic! And hosted by all your favorite Disney Friends, dressed in spectacular 20th Anniversary-only party outfits, who are hosting this star-studded event. From the skies above to the air all around, across every stage, street, and corner, glitz and glam radiate across this land of seemingly endless celebration. Get ready to fill your world with jubilation and celebration like never before, as you get closer than ever to Disney magic at the party of all parties.

Hong Kong Disneyland 20th Anniversary celebration until Jun 7, 2026, calling for all Disney fans to enjoy the party! Visit now!

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo1u12000k60t9gy7523_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

  

**All-New Anniversary-Only Castle Stage Show**

Kick things off with a bang! Get ready to bob your heads and join our hosts, Mickey and Friends, Duffy and Friends, and Disney Princesses, for a limited-time, one-year-only, electrifying celebration with music, dancing, and visual theatrics. Feel the energy of beloved Disney Friends in an exhilarating daytime performance that will leave you ready to party like never before.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo2q12000m3wcf57ACD1_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

  

**All-New “Friendtastic!” Parade**

Get the party moving! Rise to meet the excitement of our all-new, long-anticipated, and largest-ever parade, featuring 11 floats that come alive with kinetic energy, and 11 groups of beloved Disney Friends who can't wait to see you. Jump into an empowering party vibe bursting with spectacular theatrics, positive energy, and toe-tapping beats designed to get you on your feet.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo1112000k60sf6280E7_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

  

**A Special 20th Anniversary Edition of “Momentous”**

The Most Magical Show On Earth will become even more magical. With even more stories, majestic projections that extend down the entire length of Main Street U.S.A, and magically inspired drone choreography, the upgraded nighttime spectacular is the unforgettable climax to the ultimate day-to-night party.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo3o12000k60vimvD9EC_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

The Magical Party Never Stops

Dress to impress! Mickey and Friends and Duffy and Friends will appear in highly-anticipated 20th Anniversary-only outfits.

Camera ready? Capture picture-perfect moments you can't wait to share with special décor across the resort.

Indulge in crave-worthy, time-limited F&B and merchandise items, refreshed throughout the year.

Party day and night at our 3 hotels with themed décor, exhilarating activities, and enchanting hospitality.

  

  

**WORLD OF FROZEN IS NOW OPEN AT HONG KONG DISNEYLAND**

"For the First Time in Forever," immerse yourself fully in the epic world of the beloved "Frozen" films, brought to life before your very eyes!

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo4o12000dbkr5kp3464_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

**Let It Go Like Never Before at World of Frozen**

Guests are invited to explore the kingdom of Arendelle, from a magical musical boat ride to zooming through Arendelle's picturesque landscape, and Anna and Elsa's hidden forest hideaway. Indulge yourself in delicious cuisine, pick up unique souvenirs, delve deeper into the story of “Frozen” with enchanting attractions and experiences in day and night!

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo6512000dbkrmc44EE8_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo4412000cdcuzfa8539_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

**THE MOST MAGICAL SHOW ON EARTH**

The nighttime spectacular, “Momentous”, illuminates the night sky with about 20 minutes of music and memorable moments. It reminds us how precious time is, and to cherish every moment with our loved ones.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/01004120009xe630d8500_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

**CASTLE OF MAGICAL DREAMS**

Standing as a shining beacon of courage, hope and possibility, the Castle of Magical Dreams stands proudly as the new centerpiece of Hong Kong Disneyland. It is built on 13 classic Disney tales of Princesses and Queens and inspires everyone to dream big.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo4b12000bbbc7pu9690_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

**IT'S PLAYTIME WITH DUFFY AND FRIENDS**

Are you ready to jump into a whole new Fans-tasy adventure? Duffy and Friends are dressed in their seasonal outfits, and they want to write new stories with you! They love to spend this colorful time surrounded by laughter, smelling the flowers, touching the grass, bouncing around, jumping for joy, and playing wherever and whenever with you! So, let your innocent self out to play wholeheartedly.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo1t12000dbkroh5F7D3_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

**CAN'T MISS MARVEL EXPERIENCES**

If you are a Marvel fan, be sure to join the heroes in defeating the evil forces of Hydra at the highly-rated Iron Man Experience, and Ant-Man and The Wasp: Nano-Battle!

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo1q12000b74qi4v9590_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

Fantastic Dining And Shopping Experiences

Feast your eyes and satisfy your appetite with a whimsical assortment of food items inspired by classic Disney Characters or taste the exquisite cuisine integrating authentic flavors from around the world; and bring back a keepsake or two from the merchandise store to commemorate the magical experience.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo6s12000dbkrn25287F_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

Stay In The Magic

Extend the Disney spirit for a never-ending magical experience at Hong Kong Disneyland Resort hotels. Whether you are vacationing in a themed suite, spending a romantic staycation, or celebrating a spectacular day. The happiest place on earth becomes the dreami-est place, the delicious-est place, the magic-est place, with iconic Disney Friends at every turn.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo5a12000dbkrmci6D66_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo5a12000dbkr7jcD73A_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo4212000dbkr4enA56E_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

## Additional information

### Admission restrictions

Dress code

Guests over the age of 16 are not allowed to wear costumes. If the park deems the clothing to be inappropriate or may affect the play experience of other guests, the park reserves the right to refuse entry to the park or require the inappropriate clothing to be removed. Guests over the age of 16 are not allowed to wear face coverings (except for medical masks). If younger guests wear a face covering, the face covering must not obstruct peripheral vision at all times, and the position of the eyes must be completely clear and unobstructed.

Other restrictions

The park will check guests' bags when they enter the park. Drinks and chemicals in glass bottles cannot be brought into the park. Each guest is limited to bringing a small amount of food, such as a pack of biscuits and a pack of bread.

\*The above information is for reference only. Please refer to the actual information provided by the attraction.

**Join a Magical Party Like No Other at the Hong Kong Disneyland 20th Anniversary!**

On a magical island away from the rest of the world, we're throwing a party that could only happen in front of the Castle of Magical Dreams. With magic! And hosted by all your favorite Disney Friends, dressed in spectacular 20th Anniversary-only party outfits, who are hosting this star-studded event. From the skies above to the air all around, across every stage, street, and corner, glitz and glam radiate across this land of seemingly endless celebration. Get ready to fill your world with jubilation and celebration like never before, as you get closer than ever to Disney magic at the party of all parties.

Hong Kong Disneyland 20th Anniversary celebration until Jun 7, 2026, calling for all Disney fans to enjoy the party! Visit now!

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo1u12000k60t9gy7523_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

  

**All-New Anniversary-Only Castle Stage Show**

Kick things off with a bang! Get ready to bob your heads and join our hosts, Mickey and Friends, Duffy and Friends, and Disney Princesses, for a limited-time, one-year-only, electrifying celebration with music, dancing, and visual theatrics. Feel the energy of beloved Disney Friends in an exhilarating daytime performance that will leave you ready to party like never before.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo2q12000m3wcf57ACD1_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

  

**All-New “Friendtastic!” Parade**

Get the party moving! Rise to meet the excitement of our all-new, long-anticipated, and largest-ever parade, featuring 11 floats that come alive with kinetic energy, and 11 groups of beloved Disney Friends who can't wait to see you. Jump into an empowering party vibe bursting with spectacular theatrics, positive energy, and toe-tapping beats designed to get you on your feet.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo1112000k60sf6280E7_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

  

**A Special 20th Anniversary Edition of “Momentous”**

The Most Magical Show On Earth will become even more magical. With even more stories, majestic projections that extend down the entire length of Main Street U.S.A, and magically inspired drone choreography, the upgraded nighttime spectacular is the unforgettable climax to the ultimate day-to-night party.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo3o12000k60vimvD9EC_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

The Magical Party Never Stops

Dress to impress! Mickey and Friends and Duffy and Friends will appear in highly-anticipated 20th Anniversary-only outfits.

Camera ready? Capture picture-perfect moments you can't wait to share with special décor across the resort.

Indulge in crave-worthy, time-limited F&B and merchandise items, refreshed throughout the year.

Party day and night at our 3 hotels with themed décor, exhilarating activities, and enchanting hospitality.

## Hong Kong Disneyland attraction highlights

Some information may have been translated by Google Translate

**Join a Magical Party Like No Other at the Hong Kong Disneyland 20th Anniversary!**

On a magical island away from the rest of the world, we're throwing a party that could only happen in front of the Castle of Magical Dreams. With magic! And hosted by all your favorite Disney Friends, dressed in spectacular 20th Anniversary-only party outfits, who are hosting this star-studded event. From the skies above to the air all around, across every stage, street, and corner, glitz and glam radiate across this land of seemingly endless celebration. Get ready to fill your world with jubilation and celebration like never before, as you get closer than ever to Disney magic at the party of all parties.

Hong Kong Disneyland 20th Anniversary celebration until Jun 7, 2026, calling for all Disney fans to enjoy the party! Visit now!

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo1u12000k60t9gy7523_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

  

**All-New Anniversary-Only Castle Stage Show**

Kick things off with a bang! Get ready to bob your heads and join our hosts, Mickey and Friends, Duffy and Friends, and Disney Princesses, for a limited-time, one-year-only, electrifying celebration with music, dancing, and visual theatrics. Feel the energy of beloved Disney Friends in an exhilarating daytime performance that will leave you ready to party like never before.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo2q12000m3wcf57ACD1_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

  

**All-New “Friendtastic!” Parade**

Get the party moving! Rise to meet the excitement of our all-new, long-anticipated, and largest-ever parade, featuring 11 floats that come alive with kinetic energy, and 11 groups of beloved Disney Friends who can't wait to see you. Jump into an empowering party vibe bursting with spectacular theatrics, positive energy, and toe-tapping beats designed to get you on your feet.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo1112000k60sf6280E7_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

  

**A Special 20th Anniversary Edition of “Momentous”**

The Most Magical Show On Earth will become even more magical. With even more stories, majestic projections that extend down the entire length of Main Street U.S.A, and magically inspired drone choreography, the upgraded nighttime spectacular is the unforgettable climax to the ultimate day-to-night party.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo3o12000k60vimvD9EC_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

The Magical Party Never Stops

Dress to impress! Mickey and Friends and Duffy and Friends will appear in highly-anticipated 20th Anniversary-only outfits.

Camera ready? Capture picture-perfect moments you can't wait to share with special décor across the resort.

Indulge in crave-worthy, time-limited F&B and merchandise items, refreshed throughout the year.

Party day and night at our 3 hotels with themed décor, exhilarating activities, and enchanting hospitality.

  

  

**WORLD OF FROZEN IS NOW OPEN AT HONG KONG DISNEYLAND**

"For the First Time in Forever," immerse yourself fully in the epic world of the beloved "Frozen" films, brought to life before your very eyes!

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo4o12000dbkr5kp3464_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

**Let It Go Like Never Before at World of Frozen**

Guests are invited to explore the kingdom of Arendelle, from a magical musical boat ride to zooming through Arendelle's picturesque landscape, and Anna and Elsa's hidden forest hideaway. Indulge yourself in delicious cuisine, pick up unique souvenirs, delve deeper into the story of “Frozen” with enchanting attractions and experiences in day and night!

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo6512000dbkrmc44EE8_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo4412000cdcuzfa8539_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

**THE MOST MAGICAL SHOW ON EARTH**

The nighttime spectacular, “Momentous”, illuminates the night sky with about 20 minutes of music and memorable moments. It reminds us how precious time is, and to cherish every moment with our loved ones.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/01004120009xe630d8500_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

**CASTLE OF MAGICAL DREAMS**

Standing as a shining beacon of courage, hope and possibility, the Castle of Magical Dreams stands proudly as the new centerpiece of Hong Kong Disneyland. It is built on 13 classic Disney tales of Princesses and Queens and inspires everyone to dream big.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo4b12000bbbc7pu9690_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

**IT'S PLAYTIME WITH DUFFY AND FRIENDS**

Are you ready to jump into a whole new Fans-tasy adventure? Duffy and Friends are dressed in their seasonal outfits, and they want to write new stories with you! They love to spend this colorful time surrounded by laughter, smelling the flowers, touching the grass, bouncing around, jumping for joy, and playing wherever and whenever with you! So, let your innocent self out to play wholeheartedly.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo1t12000dbkroh5F7D3_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

**CAN'T MISS MARVEL EXPERIENCES**

If you are a Marvel fan, be sure to join the heroes in defeating the evil forces of Hydra at the highly-rated Iron Man Experience, and Ant-Man and The Wasp: Nano-Battle!

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo1q12000b74qi4v9590_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

Fantastic Dining And Shopping Experiences

Feast your eyes and satisfy your appetite with a whimsical assortment of food items inspired by classic Disney Characters or taste the exquisite cuisine integrating authentic flavors from around the world; and bring back a keepsake or two from the merchandise store to commemorate the magical experience.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo6s12000dbkrn25287F_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

Stay In The Magic

Extend the Disney spirit for a never-ending magical experience at Hong Kong Disneyland Resort hotels. Whether you are vacationing in a themed suite, spending a romantic staycation, or celebrating a spectacular day. The happiest place on earth becomes the dreami-est place, the delicious-est place, the magic-est place, with iconic Disney Friends at every turn.

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo5a12000dbkrmci6D66_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

![](https://dimg04.tripcdn.com/images/1lo5a12000dbkr7jcD73A_W_1024_10000_Q80.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)

## Additional information

### Admission restrictions

Dress code

Guests over the age of 16 are not allowed to wear costumes. If the park deems the clothing to be inappropriate or may affect the play experience of other guests, the park reserves the right to refuse entry to the park or require the inappropriate clothing to be removed. Guests over the age of 16 are not allowed to wear face coverings (except for medical masks). If younger guests wear a face covering, the face covering must not obstruct peripheral vision at all times, and the position of the eyes must be completely clear and unobstructed.

Other restrictions

The park will check guests' bags when they enter the park. Drinks and chemicals in glass bottles cannot be brought into the park. Each guest is limited to bringing a small amount of food, such as a pack of biscuits and a pack of bread.

\*The above information is for reference only. Please refer to the actual information provided by the attraction.

Additional Capabilities\n\n# Locations, Destinations and Categories\nContent Discovery with the API\n\n## \nOverview\nBuilding great customer journeys starts with helping users find exactly what they’re looking for, quickly, intuitively, and with minimal friction. That’s why we provide a suite of powerful content discovery endpoints to help you deliver personalized and well-organized travel experiences across any platform.\nWhether you're creating a travel booking app, a city tourism portal, or a B2B reseller platform, our **Destinations** , **Locations** , and **Categories** APIs help structure and filter content so your users can explore effortlessly.\n\n...\n\n### \n#### \nWhat It Does\nReturns a list of more granular _locations_ where experiences take place. Think individual attractions, museums, venues, or parks.\nCommon Use Cases\n* Displaying exact location info on product detail pages.\n* Enabling “near me” searches for mobile users using GPS-based filtering.\n* Showing products on a map view or geo-based clustering feature.\nReal-World Scenario\nImagine a mobile travel app where a user enables geolocation. You can use `/locations` to fetch all venues within a certain radius of the user's current coordinates, allowing spontaneous bookings like “Skip-the-Line at the Van Gogh Museum – 100m away”.\n\n...\n\nWhat It Does\nReturns a structured list of categories that group your product offerings into themes like “Museums”, “Boat Tours”, or “Day Trips”.\nCommon Use Cases\n* Adding category filters to product listings or search UIs.\n* Organizing catalog pages, such as `/categories/tours` .\n* Letting users browse products by interest.\nReal-World Scenario\nLet’s say a user visits your app and filters by “Outdoor Activities”. Behind the scenes, you’re using the categories endpoint to populate these options dynamically, making your UI easier to maintain and future-proof as more experiences are added."],"source_id":"search_8e953b7719e1425fa15a3a4e0fa6c3ed#2"},{"url":"https://developers.trip.com/","title":"Trip.com Developers","excerpts":["# Your Trip Starts Here\n* [](https://www.trip.com/)\n* [](https://www.ctrip.com/)\n* [](https://www.skyscanner.net/)\n* [](https://www.qunar.com/)\n\n...\n\n## Contact Us\n### About\n* [News](https://www.trip.com/newsroom/?locale=en-xx)\n* [Privacy Statement](https://pages.trip.com/service-guideline/privacy-policy-en-xx.html)\n* [Careers](https://careers.trip.com/)\nCopyright @2022 Trip.com Travel Singapore Pte. This Hong Kong Disneyland ticket includes all the benefits of a Silver Membership with additional days of park access. It also offers greater flexibility in choosing visit days.\nPlatinum Magic Access comes with unlimited access to the park throughout the year with no blockout dates. This Hong Kong Disneyland ticket includes everything that comes with Gold Membership, maximum flexibility with no blockout days, and additional exclusive offers and events access.\nFor the latest details on Magic Access membership types and Hong Kong Disneyland ticket prices, visiting Hong Kong Disneyland's [official website](https://www.hongkongdisneyland.com/) is recommended.\n[__ Book Special Hong Kong Disneyland Tickets Now! __](https://www.trip.com/travel-guide/attraction/hong-kong/hong-kong-disneyland-10558849/)\n\n## Must-visit attractions in Hong Kong Disneyland\nCinderella Carousel at night in Hong Kong Disneyland. Photo by Jay R on Unsplash\nHong Kong Disneyland offers a unique blend of attractions combining classic Disney magic with distinct cultural elements. Here’s a list of some must-visit attractions:\nMystic Manor (Mystic Point): A unique take on the Haunted Mansion found in other Disney parks, it features magical artifacts that come to life instead of ghosts in an enchanting, family-friendly adventure. The ride uses trackless technology and makes each experience unique.\nBig Grizzly Mountain Runaway Mine Cars (Grizzly Gulch): It’s a thrilling roller coaster ride that combines the excitement of Big Thunder Mountain and the Everest expedition. The ride takes through a gold mine with surprises along the way.\n\n...\n\n## What to pack for a day at Hong Kong Disneyland?\nHong Kong Disneyland trip is an exciting experience. 129:## Other visitors' reviews of Hong Kong Disneyland
139:On my fourth trip to Hong Kong, I finally set foot on the land of Hong Kong Disneyland and spent a magical day alone (though it was also quite tiring). Getting there from my Wan Chai hotel involved one tram and two subway rides, taking about an hour – a bit of a hassle, but overall manageable. I went on a Saturday, and bought my tickets, early admission pass, and three-in-one meal voucher the day before, for a little over 1000 RMB. I did my research beforehand, and even though it was a weekend and crowded, everything went smoothly, and I had a great time.

*   [![Image 191: user-icon](https://ak-d.tripcdn.com/images/27c6n12000na9jeqj71E2_C_100_100_Q50.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)](https://us.trip.com/travel-guide/attraction/hong-kong/hong-kong-disneyland-10558849/)M25***43   5.0/5   Outstanding Original text   [I took my kids to Hong Kong Disneyland 10 times and made a true evaluation of Hong Kong Disneyland. 1. You must download the Hong Kong Disneyland APP in advance to check the queue time for performances. I have been to Hong Kong Disneyland at different time periods. Sometimes there are very few people in Hong Kong Disneyland. Most projects only take 5-10 minutes. You can experience VIP. Of course, sometimes I have queued for more than an hour. 2. Hong Kong Disneyland is very hot outside in summer. You must be prepared to prevent heatstroke and cool down. Some projects are queued outside. It is really hot, and it is very cold inside. It is not a big problem when there are many people. When there are few people, it is really cold and gives you goose bumps. You must bring a thin coat when you bring your baby 3. The staff everywhere can speak English, Mandarin, and Cantonese, so you don't have to worry about the language problem. However, some performances, such as Disney Magic Book House, Mickey Fantasia, and The Lion King, are mainly in Cantonese. If you don't understand, just watch it. Children like it very much (look at the time and queue up at least ten minutes in advance, otherwise you can only queue for the next show if there are too many people) 4. Regarding food, the consumption inside is quite high, but you can bring your own food, such as bread, chocolate, etc. She will open the bag and check it when you enter the park. Just don't bring food with smell. Also, you must bring water. There are several toilets inside that can be connected to tap water and can be drunk directly. If you eat a children's meal in the park, you will usually get a glass of water, which is 30 yuan per bottle of mineral water. You should bring your own water. 5. Regarding playing, those with children must push a stroller by themselves. You can walk 10,000 to 20,000 steps a day. Sometimes you have to queue, which is also very tiring for the children. Once you enter, you will see the American town street. You can go left or right. After playing around, you will return to the starting point. It is just right to watch the fireworks at night.](https://us.trip.com/travel-guide/attraction/hong-kong/hong-kong-disneyland-10558849/) Show more           4  Reviewed on October 10, 2024  

*   [![Image 192: user-icon](https://ak-d.tripcdn.com/images/27c0712000na9ji5b4486_C_100_100_Q50.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)](https://us.trip.com/travel-guide/attraction/hong-kong/hong-kong-disneyland-10558849/)M85***04   5.0/5   Outstanding Original text   [The park generally includes 8 theme areas (8 in California, 7 each in Florida, Tokyo and Shanghai, and 5 in Paris), similar to other Disney parks, including "Main Street, U.S.A.", "Toy Story," "Adventureland," "Fantasyland," "Tomorrowland," "Grizzly Gulch," "Toy Story," "Mystic Manor," and "Frozen World." In addition to the well-known classic Disney stories and rides, Hong Kong Disneyland also conceives some rides, entertainment performances and parades designed specifically for Hong Kong in line with Hong Kong's cultural characteristics. Disney cartoon characters such as Mickey Mouse, Winnie the Pooh, Mulan, Cinderella, and Sleeping Beauty can also be found in the park.](https://us.trip.com/travel-guide/attraction/hong-kong/hong-kong-disneyland-10558849/) Show more       3  Reviewed on December 3, 2024

## Additional information

### Admission restrictions

Dress code

Guests over the age of 16 are not allowed to wear costumes. If the park deems the clothing to be inappropriate or may affect the play experience of other guests, the park reserves the right to refuse entry to the park or require the inappropriate clothing to be removed. Guests over the age of 16 are not allowed to wear face coverings (except for medical masks). If younger guests wear a face covering, the face covering must not obstruct peripheral vision at all times, and the position of the eyes must be completely clear and unobstructed.

Other restrictions

The park will check guests' bags when they enter the park. Drinks and chemicals in glass bottles cannot be brought into the park. Each guest is limited to bringing a small amount of food, such as a pack of biscuits and a pack of bread.

*The above information is for reference only. Please refer to the actual information provided by the attraction.

_󰄢_ Luggage storage

It starts around 8:30 PM and combines projections, lasers, water screens, lights, and fireworks—super impressive! The story weaves together "time" and "memories," with Disney characters appearing one after another, including The Lion King, Frozen, Toy Story… by the end, I was really touched🥹 I actually cried😭 I recommend securing a spot at least 30 minutes early, ideally right in front of the castle to see the full effect! 🌿 Explorers Lodge This hotel is perfect for families or friends traveling together, with an overall adventure + nature theme, featuring decorations inspired by Africa, Asia, South America, and more, giving a strong vacation vibe🌍 The rooms are spacious and comfortable, with a partial sea view from the window. There are many photo spots in the public areas, plus an outdoor pool and kids’ activities. Although the rooms don’t feel brand new, the stay is very relaxing! We happened to be celebrating a birthday, so we also booked a birthday gift🎂 🧺 For dinner, since we bought the fireworks VIP package (which reserves a spot to watch the fireworks), we ate at the buffet inside the park! There are many options (both Western and Chinese), and the quality was better than expected👍 But since the whole package isn’t cheap, I suggest booking it only for special occasions😂 🌟 Quick tip: Be sure to download the official Disney app—it’s super convenient for checking ride wait times & show schedules💪🏼 Besides the street shows, I highly recommend watching The Lion King and Mickey’s PhilharMagic story theater! Remember to take photos of the castle both during the day and at night—the lighting difference is huge, and every shot looks like a postcard! The park has undergone significant changes in recent years, including the addition of the Frozen-themed area. This time, I found the experience truly suitable for all ages. Special discounts for seniors and free admission for toddlers make it both affordable and enjoyable! Located in Lantau Island, Hong Kong Disneyland offers convenient transportation and an exceptional resort atmosphere. Whether it's sunny or rainy, the Western-style architecture provides perfect photo opportunities. The newly added "World of Frozen" faithfully recreates scenes from the movie, making every corner a photo-worthy spot. Kids get excited just seeing their favorite Disney characters as the whole family steps into the magical world of the park. Recommended itinerary: Start at the park entrance and take a photo at Mickey's Garden. Then head to Fantasyland to enjoy attractions like The Many Adventures of Winnie the Pooh, Cinderella Carousel, and the latest hit "World of Frozen." For a gentler experience, ride "It's a Small World," which is perfect for both seniors and kids. Finally, visit Tomorrowland for Hyperspace Mountain and interactive games with Marvel heroes—fun for all ages. Must-visit photo spots: · Mickey's Garden at the park entrance and train station (a must for photos!) · Daytime or nighttime parades · World of Frozen—Elsa's Castle and Anna's Cottage · The park's iconic Castle of Magical Dreams · Every corner of Main Street U.S.A. exudes a European vibe, perfect for photos Best attractions for seniors and kids: · "It's a Small World" (a slow ride for kids to enjoy) · Disney Friends Meet-and-Greet Parade (no need to queue for photos) · "Frozen Ever After" boat ride in World of Frozen · Stage and lake performances—arrive early for front-row seats · Hyperspace Mountain/Glow-in-the-Dark Parade—high-energy atmosphere · Mickey-shaped ice cream bars (a treat for both grandparents and kids) Tips for seniors and toddlers: 1. Tickets for seniors aged 60+ and JoyYou Card holders are only $100, while children under 3 enter for free—great value for grandparents bringing their grandchildren. 2. For popular attractions like World of Frozen, arrive early or use the mobile app to reserve spots. 3. Some paths may be slippery during rain; bring rain gear. Indoor attractions offer shelter. 4. Consider bringing a stroller for kids under 3 to ease the burden on parents. Stroller rentals are available at the park entrance. 5. Air conditioning can be strong, and rainy weather can be humid (especially in park shops), so dress appropriately. Important notes: · The park's general opening hours are 10:00/10:30 AM to 8:30/9:00 PM. Arrive on time to make the most of your day. · Bring a water bottle; there are multiple water fountains in the park. · Crowds are larger on holidays or during peak seasons. Use the Disneyland mobile app to plan your route and maximize your experience. · The park offers various restaurants and buffets with moderate prices to suit different budgets. This trip was relaxing for both seniors and kids. Grandparents can relive childhood memories while kids meet their favorite cartoon characters. It's truly a place where generations grow together. Rain or shine, the park offers beautiful scenery and great photo opportunities, making it a perfect family outing! 旅行跑馬燈 __ 10 ![Image 200: author](https://ak-d.tripcdn.com/images/0a24w224x97yewu4kA4CC_C_30_30_Q70.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)](https://us.trip.com/moments/detail/hong-kong-38-143129324/)

*   [![Image 205: 3 Best Rides at Hong Kong Disneyland](https://ak-d.tripcdn.com/images/1mi0c12000cyfpos37ED7_W_640_0_Q70.webp?proc=source/trip&proc=source%2ftrip) 3 Best Rides at Hong Kong Disneyland Visiting Hong Kong Disneyland is an enchanting experience that brings out the inner child in everyone. With its unique blend of Disney magic and Chinese culture, the park offers a plethora of attractions and rides that cater to all ages. Let me introduce you to three of the favorite rides at Hong Kong Disneyland. 1. Hyperspace Mountain: Step into the Star Wars universe and embark on an intergalactic adventure aboard this thrilling roller coaster. Hyperspace Mountain takes you on a high-speed journey through space, complete with immersive visuals and exhilarating twists and turns. It's a must-try for all Star Wars fans and adrenaline junkies alike. 2. Mystic Manor: Prepare to be amazed as you enter the enchanting world of Lord Henry Mystic and his mischievous monkey, Albert. This unique dark ride takes you on a captivating journey through a mysterious museum filled with magical artifacts. With stunning special effects and an original musical score, Mystic Manor is a favorite among visitors seeking a more immersive and enchanting experience. 3. Jungle River Cruise: Embark on a classic adventure as you set sail on the Jungle River Cruise. This guided boat tour takes you through lush landscapes, ancient ruins, and encounters with animatronic animals. The witty and entertaining skippers add a touch of humor to the experience, making it an enjoyable ride for the whole family. These are just a few of the many incredible rides and attractions that await you at Hong Kong Disneyland. Whether you're seeking thrills, enchantment, or family-friendly fun, the park offers something for everyone. So, grab your Mickey ears and get ready for a magical adventure that will create memories to last a lifetime. *   [![Image 207: Honest Advice from Former Hong Kong Disneyland Staff!](https://ak-d.tripcdn.com/images/1mi3x12000rymlntpBF56_W_640_0_Q70.webp?proc=source/trip&proc=source%2ftrip) Honest Advice from Former Hong Kong Disneyland Staff! At the end of March, during Hong Kong Disneyland's 20th Anniversary Celebration, the Duffy and Friends Spring Sail event (3.20-6.7) is also ongoing. Here’s a genuine and well-founded guide—ladies, bookmark it if you need! ♦️Tip 1: Park Entry Time and Ride Order The park opens from 10:30 AM to 8:30 PM, but it’s recommended to arrive for security check before 9:30 AM. For the first group entering in the morning, it’s best to head straight to “Frozen Ever After.” If you enter a bit later after ticket scanning, start with “Hyperspace Mountain” or “Iron Man Experience” in Tomorrowland. ♦️Tip 2: Gear Checklist Prepare before you go: ID card, empty water bottle, 3C-certified power bank, filling sealed snacks, folding umbrella or raincoat, tissues, and wear comfortable sneakers. ♦️Tip 3: Prohibited Items at Security Selfie sticks, tripods, folding chairs, glass containers, drinks over 650ml, sprays, luggage over 22 inches, food that needs heating, and alcoholic beverages are strictly forbidden. ♦️Tip 4: Security Lane Choice Use the middle lane at security check for faster processing and to save time entering the park. ♦️Tip 5: Direct Route to Frozen Ever After To be the first to rush into “Frozen Ever After,” follow this route: Main Gate → Main Street, U.S.A. → Right side of the Castle → Fantasyland → Frozen Ever After. The clock tower in Arendelle Kingdom chimes familiar tunes on the hour—don’t forget to take photos. ♦️Tip 6: Birthday Month Freebies If it’s your birthday month, go to the Town Hall on Main Street, U.S.A. after entering to get a birthday badge. Wearing it will get you special birthday wishes from the staff! ♦️Tip 7: Parade Viewing Spots On March 27, the biggest parade in the 20th anniversary history, the “Disney Friends Springtime Carnival,” will take place! Featuring 11 floats and over 30 Disney friends. Recommended viewing spot: along Main Street, U.S.A. Arrive 20-30 minutes early to secure a good spot. ♦️Tip 8: Must-Do Attractions 🎯 Frozen Ever After (Frozen Ever After): Elsa’s “Let It Go” performance is breathtaking 🎯 Big Grizzly Mountain Runaway Mine Cars (Grizzly Gulch): Unique to Hong Kong Disneyland! 🎯 Mystic Manor (Mystic Point): The world’s only trackless electromagnetic vehicle adventure 🎯 Iron Man Experience (Tomorrowland): 4D flying simulation 🎯 Hyperspace Mountain (Tomorrowland): Indoor roller coaster 🎯 RC Racer (Toy Story Land): U-shaped track ♦️Tip 9: Height Restrictions Reminder 🎯 Big Grizzly Mountain Runaway Mine Cars: 112cm and above 🎯 RC Racer: 120cm and above 🎯 Hyperspace Mountain: Recommended 102cm and above 🎯 Iron Man Experience: Recommended 102cm and above 📌Special Reminder March weather: temperatures around 22-26°C, warm and comfortable, with possible showers—bring a folding umbrella. Dress suggestion: wear light colors (pink/white/blue) to match the Spring Sail theme perfectly. *   [![Image 211: Hong Kong Disneyland: A Magical Adventure](https://ak-d.tripcdn.com/images/1mi6g224x95t9e4e8EDFE_W_640_0_Q70.webp?proc=source/trip&proc=source%2ftrip) * 香港迪士尼 * 夢幻煙火秀 * 樂園行程攻略 * 家庭親子遊 * 旅遊小貼士 Hong Kong Disneyland: A Magical Adventure This time, we recommend a trip to the must-visit dreamland for Hong Kong locals—Hong Kong Disneyland! If you're looking for a place in the city to escape reality and indulge in your dreams, this is the perfect choice. With its popular themed areas, all-inclusive tickets for unlimited fun, and the grand finale "Disney in the Stars Fireworks Show," it's definitely worth arriving early and enjoying the park from day to night! 🎢 Highlights of the Trip Hong Kong Disneyland not only features classic attractions from around the world but also offers performances and cuisine with local flair. From fairytale castles to thrilling adventures, every area is full of surprises. This guide focuses on the latest and most touching "Disney in the Stars Fireworks Show," teaching you how to secure the best viewing spots and immerse yourself in the fairytale atmosphere under the fireworks. It also includes comprehensive tips on tickets, dining, and more! 📍 Hong Kong Disneyland Address: Hong Kong Disneyland Resort, Lantau Island, Hong Kong Opening Hours: October 12: 10:00 AM - 8:30 PM; October 13: 10:30 AM - 8:00 PM Tickets: HKD 548 💕 Recommended Attractions & Practical Tips 1. Fairytale Castle (Main Viewing Area for Fireworks Show) It is recommended to arrive at least 30 minutes early around the Fantasyland Castle to secure a spot right in front. This area offers a wide view for the entire fireworks show and light projections, allowing you to fully immerse yourself in a fairytale night! The program features classic Disney characters, music synchronized with fireworks and projections, creating stunning visuals and a perfect atmosphere. Highly recommend capturing panoramic videos with your phone for memories! 2. Tomorrowland and Adventureland Classic Attractions (Morning Priority) In the morning, start with the less crowded themed areas like Tomorrowland and Adventureland. Attractions such as "Iron Man Experience," "Buzz Lightyear Astro Blasters," and "Jungle River Cruise" are great for avoiding peak queues. These rides are suitable for both kids and adults, combining adventure and fun with educational elements. 3. Dining Recommendations: Cinderella Café and Royal Banquet Hall Cinderella Café specializes in Western-style set meals, while the Royal Banquet Hall is known for its diverse international cuisine, offering Chinese, Japanese, and buffet options. Choose between dining in or grabbing a quick takeaway meal based on your preferences and schedule. 🗣️ "Disney in the Stars Fireworks Show" Review & Tips The fireworks show is undoubtedly the highlight of the day! You'll truly experience the magic of "entering with dreams, leaving with memories." The music and lights synchronized with the fireworks create a perfect atmosphere. Pro tip: Arrive at the main castle area 30 minutes early to secure a spot. The show lasts about 20 minutes, so if it's crowded, bring a hat or a small mat to sit on while waiting. Before the show starts, the park will broadcast safety reminders, so be patient and avoid pushing through the crowd to prevent congestion. ❗ Must-Have Essentials: Make sure to fully charge your power bank and bring a camera or phone, as the nighttime light effects at the main castle are stunning for photos! A jacket and umbrella are also practical, as the temperature drops in the evening, and occasional light rain adds to the fairytale vibe. 🚄 Transportation Tips Take the MTR Tung Chung Line to Sunny Bay Station and transfer to the Disneyland Resort Line. The station exit leads directly to the park entrance, making transportation incredibly convenient! If driving, you can park at the official Disneyland parking lot. It's recommended to book tickets and confirm your schedule in advance on platforms like trip.com. 🍰 Food Tips Don't miss the nostalgic popcorn and Mickey-shaped ice cream—enjoying these treats while strolling around is pure happiness! Park restaurants tend to get crowded during dinner hours, so try to avoid peak times or use online reservation services. 呂學舜 __ 43 ![Image 212: author](https://ak-d.tripcdn.com/images/0a236224x95ct19gy0A9C_C_30_30_Q70.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)](https://us.trip.com/moments/detail/hong-kong-38-136789172/)

Tomorrowland Zone. Highlight - Iron Man Rating - 10/10 2. Toy Story Zone Highlight - Soldier Drop We only rode this one once in this zone because the other ride was scary 😆 Rating - 9/10 3. Frozen Zone Highlight - Every ride!!! Especially the boat ride, it’s so much fun. Worth paying for the fast pass at 129 HKD. Rating - 100/10 There are many other zones in Disneyland where you can choose rides you like, including those for kids, thrilling rides for adults, and cute ones. *   [![Image 215: Hong Kong Disneyland | Duffy and Friends' Adorable Spring Adventure Begins!](https://ak-d.tripcdn.com/images/1mi2j12000sar4nlb756E_W_640_0_Q70.webp?proc=source/trip&proc=source%2ftrip) Hong Kong Disneyland | Duffy and Friends' Adorable Spring Adventure Begins! Black Diamond Release AlexanderCarmichael __ 5 ![Image 216: author](https://ak-d.tripcdn.com/images/1mi4512000dclvu4h6293_C_30_30_Q70.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)](https://us.trip.com/moments/detail/hong-kong-38-144896221/)
*   [![Image 217: Hong Kong Disneyland without queues!](https://ak-d.tripcdn.com/images/1mi3f224x98p7ewinD5CE_W_640_0_Q70.webp?proc=source/trip&proc=source%2ftrip) Hong Kong Disneyland without queues! In 2025, Hong Kong Disneyland celebrated its 20th anniversary! To mark this milestone, the park has organized numerous events, including a new show, themed decorations, 11 stunning parade floats, exclusive souvenirs, and much more! When planning our trip, we decided to take a 2-day transit in Hong Kong to enjoy the childhood magic in one of the coolest parks. If you're also planning a transit in Hong Kong, here are my tips: 1. Stay at one of the Disney hotels. We chose Hollywood Hotel because it's the most recently renovated. Staying at a hotel in the park is a unique experience! You'll find magic at every step: Mickey-shaped pancakes for breakfast, Goofy walking around the hotel hugging kids, and Disney-themed slippers! 2. Get a 2-day park pass. Since Hong Kong Disneyland has been open for quite some time, it has transformed into a lush tropical jungle. There’s plenty of shade and picturesque spots for photos, making it a pleasure to stroll around. Taking your time to enjoy the park is ideal, and a 2-day ticket is the perfect solution. We arrived at the park in the evening, explored, rode some attractions, watched the parade, and enjoyed the light and laser show. 3. Opt for early entry on the second day. This was our best decision! The park officially opens at 10 AM, but with early entry, you can get in at 9 AM. As a result, we managed to ride all the attractions in Fantasyland without waiting a single minute. Afterward, we headed to the Frozen zone, where we rode the attractions twice without queues. When the park officially opened and crowds rushed to the popular spots, we leisurely moved around the park, avoiding long lines! Have a great time!🌷 Nata and Alex __ 5 ![Image 218: author](https://ak-d.tripcdn.com/images/0a25i224x98prf7w5FDB7_C_30_30_Q70.webp?proc=source%2ftrip)](https://us.trip.com/moments/detail/hong-kong-38-143284024/)
